#### <span id="page-77-3"></span>**21.7.13.3.9.2 (10-01-2025)**

#### **Other EIN Research Requests**

Taxpayers or their authorized representatives may contact the IRS to confirm (verify) the taxpayer's EIN or request a copy of the original CP 575, Notice of New Employer Identification Number. These requests (1)

could include, but are not limited to, an EIN that was lost, misplaced, or forgotten. If the taxpayer asks for a duplicate CP 575, send Letter 147C, EIN Previously Assigned. Explain the original notice of EIN assignment cannot be duplicated. See IRM 21.7.1.4.7.1, Employer Identification Number (EIN) Verification and Requests for Letter 147C, EIN Previously Assigned, for guidance.

<span id="page-78-0"></span>**Note:** For guidance regarding the status of a Form SS-4 application, see IRM 21.7.13.3.9.1, Form SS-4 Application Status.

#### **21.7.13.4 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Determining Whether an Entity Needs an EIN**

- Before assigning a new EIN, always perform research using the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to determine whether an EIN is needed. This subsection contains procedures for: (1)
  - Handling taxpayer inquiries about whether an EIN is needed
  - Performing research to ensure that a taxpayer does not already have an EIN
  - Entering search criteria
  - Research Command Codes
  - Research using Command Code ENMOD
  - Actions to take if an EIN is found
  - Resolving duplicate EINs
  - Reactivating an EIN
  - Taxpayer claims they did not request an EIN
  - Determining whether a new EIN is needed when the ownership/classification of an entity changes and
  - EINs required for business purposes

<span id="page-78-1"></span>**Note:** Manually input the appropriate research CC's when the IAT EIN Assignment Tool is unavailable.

#### <span id="page-78-2"></span>**21.7.13.4.1 (03-13-2017)**

#### **Responding to Taxpayer Inquiries**

Use the information in the table below to determine whether a new EIN is needed, based on a taxpayer inquiry. (1)

<span id="page-79-0"></span>

| If                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>The<br>taxpayer<br>previously had<br>an<br>EIN<br>for<br>the<br>same<br>entity<br>2)<br>The<br>taxpayer<br>is<br>incorporating<br>using<br>the<br>same<br>name<br>and<br>in<br>the<br>same<br>state<br>as<br>another<br>corporation<br>whose<br>filing<br>requirements<br>have<br>been<br>closed | The<br>same<br>EIN<br>is<br>used.<br>Issue<br>a<br>new<br>EIN<br>if<br>the<br>inquiry was<br>submitted<br>in<br>writing<br>via<br>correspondence.<br>If<br>the<br>inquiry was<br>received<br>from<br>toll<br>free<br>phones,<br>advise<br>the<br>caller<br>to<br>submit<br>a<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>by fax<br>or<br>mail.<br>Note:<br>Research<br>the<br>previous<br>corporation's<br>account<br>for<br>cancellation<br>of<br>filing |
| 3)<br>The<br>taxpayer<br>is<br>incorporating<br>using<br>the<br>same<br>name<br>and<br>in<br>the<br>same<br>state<br>as<br>another<br>corporation<br>with<br>open<br>filing<br>requirements                                                                                                            | requirements.<br>a.<br>Check<br>to<br>see<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>the<br>same<br>corporation.<br>b.<br>If<br>not,<br>ask<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>to<br>produce<br>proof<br>of<br>incorporation<br>(articles<br>of<br>incorporation)<br>and<br>submit<br>a<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>with<br>articles<br>of<br>incorporation/organization<br>by fax<br>or<br>mail.                                                                            |
| 4)<br>A<br>bank<br>will<br>not<br>accept<br>the<br>taxpayer's<br>EIN<br>because<br>another<br>taxpayer<br>has<br>a<br>number<br>exactly like<br>it                                                                                                                                                     | Do<br>not<br>issue<br>an<br>EIN.<br>Note:<br>Banks<br>do<br>not<br>use<br>dashes<br>to<br>distinguish<br>EINs<br>from<br>SSNs.<br>It<br>is<br>the<br>responsibility of<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>to<br>contact<br>the<br>bank<br>to<br>settle<br>the<br>issue.                                                                                                                                                                       |

#### <span id="page-79-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.2 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Researching Taxpayer Information**

- To avoid any possibility of duplication, when you receive a request for an EIN, always perform thorough research using the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to verify that an EIN has not previously been assigned. (1)
- <span id="page-79-2"></span>Research command codes, NAMEI (Individual Master File IMF) and NAMEB (BMF), can be manually input when the tool is unavailable. **Note:** For complete instructions for using command codes, refer to the IDRS Command Codes Job Aid located on SERP. (2)

#### <span id="page-79-3"></span>**21.7.13.4.2.1 (03-13-2017)**

#### **Entering Search Criteria**

- When using the IAT EIN Assignment Tool or any of the command codes described in this subsection (when the tool is unavailable), research the entity thoroughly for: (1)
  - All names of the owners, such as partners (e.g., Smith & Jones, Jones & Smith, Smith and Jones)
  - Spelling variations, such as one word versus two words (e.g., Safe Guard and Safeguard)
  - Name of business with punctuation and without (e.g., A–B–C–D and ABCD and A B C D)
  - Incorporated or formation information in the State provided on Line 9b.
  - The taxpayer's name and mailing ZIP code. Begin with the first three digits of the mailing ZIP code and then expand your search to five. (If nothing is found, use the location ZIP code, first three digits and then expand your search to five.)
- <span id="page-80-0"></span>If you cannot locate an account, always verify you have input the information correctly before proceeding. (2)

### **21.7.13.4.2.2 (12-18-2015)**

# **Research Using Command Codes (CC) NAMEI, NAMEB, NAMEE, AND NAMES**

- The IAT EIN Assignment Tool performs research using CCs NAMEI, NAMEB, NAMEE, to determine if an EIN has already been assigned. This tool must be used for research when available. Use various elements of the search criteria (parameters) to research the entity thoroughly. For example: (1)
  - Primary name
  - DBA name
  - Combinations of state
  - Zip code (first three digits initially and expand to five)
  - Street address

See IRM 2.3.60, Command Codes NAMES, NAMEE, NAMEI, NAMEB, FINDS, and FINDE, for additional information.

When the IAT EIN Assignment tool is unavailable, research the entity using the Name Search Facility (NSF) with the correct command code as described in the table below. Use same search criteria as shown in paragraph 1 above. (2)

| If<br>you<br>are<br>searching for<br>an<br>account<br>with |                       |
|------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------|
| an                                                         | Then<br>use           |
| 1)<br>EIN<br>already assigned                              | CC<br>NAMEB,          |
|                                                            | NAMEE                 |
| 2)<br>SSN/IRSN/ITIN                                        | CC<br>NAMEI,<br>NAMES |

#### <span id="page-81-0"></span>**21.7.13.4.2.3 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Using CC ENMOD (Taxpayer Information File)**

If it appears that the taxpayer already has an EIN, use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to perform research. If the tool is unavailable, use CC ENMOD and other command codes shown in IRM 3.13.5.99, Command Codes Used for Researching EINs, to research. (1)

#### <span id="page-81-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.2.4 (10-01-2025)**

### **If an EIN is Found/Not Found**

After researching for a previously assigned EIN using the IAT EIN Assignment tool (or the correct research command codes if the tool is unavailable), use the information in the table below to determine the correct action to take. (1)

| If                                           | Then                                                |
|----------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>A<br>previously assigned<br>EIN        | Assign<br>an<br>EIN,<br>using<br>the<br>correct     |

|                                              | Domestic<br>Entities.                               |
| 2)<br>A<br>previously assigned<br>EIN        | Reactivate<br>the<br>EIN<br>using<br>TC<br>000      |
| is<br>found,<br>but<br>the<br>EIN<br>dropped | procedures<br>in<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.6,           |
| off<br>Master<br>File<br>due<br>to           | Reactivating<br>an<br>EIN<br>(TC<br>000).           |
| inactivity.                                  |                                                     |

| If                                                                                                                                                                         | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 3)<br>A<br>previously assigned<br>EIN<br>Is<br>found,<br>and<br>A<br>change<br>in<br>entity<br>classification,<br>status,<br>and/or<br>ownership<br>is<br>indicated        | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.3,<br>Entity<br>Classification<br>and<br>Ownership<br>Changes.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| 4)<br>A<br>previously assigned<br>EIN<br>is<br>found<br>for<br>a<br>mailed<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>and<br>there<br>are<br>no<br>changes<br>in<br>entity type<br>or<br>ownership | Notate<br>the<br>previously assigned<br>EIN<br>on<br>Form<br>SS-4,<br>followed<br>by PA<br>(previously<br>assigned)<br>to<br>indicate<br>a<br>new<br>number<br>was<br>not<br>assigned.<br>Send<br>Letter<br>147C,<br>EIN<br>Previously Assigned,<br>to<br>the<br>address<br>of<br>record<br>to<br>notify the<br>taxpayer<br>of<br>a<br>previously assigned<br>number.<br>Note:<br>If<br>the<br>address<br>on<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>differs<br>from<br>the<br>address<br>of<br>record,<br>refer<br>to<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.6.5.1,<br>Changing<br>an<br>Address.<br>Exception:<br>Do<br>not<br>send<br>if<br>research<br>shows<br>Letter<br>147C<br>was<br>sent<br>within<br>the<br>last<br>30<br>days.<br>Do<br>not<br>send<br>if<br>research<br>shows<br>the<br>EIN<br>was<br>assigned<br>within<br>the<br>last<br>30<br>days<br>as<br>a<br>CP<br>575<br>was<br>generated<br>during<br>the<br>assignment<br>process.<br>Do<br>not<br>fax<br>the<br>previously assigned<br>EIN<br>back<br>to<br>a<br>third<br>party designee.<br>Their<br>authority is<br>to<br>obtain<br>newly assigned<br>EINs<br>only.<br>Reminder:<br>Faxed<br>Forms<br>SS-4<br>are<br>worked<br>in<br>PEGA.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.8,<br>Introduction<br>to<br>Enterprise<br>File<br>Storage<br>(EFS)<br>PEGA. |
| 5)<br>If<br>a<br>previously assigned<br>EIN                                                                                                                                | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.3.9.1,<br>Form<br>SS-4                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| is<br>found<br>during<br>a<br>phone<br>call                                                                                                                                | Application<br>Status,<br>for<br>guidance.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 6)<br>Two<br>EINs<br>are<br>found                                                                                                                                          | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.6.3,<br>Resolving<br>Multiple<br>EINs<br>(CC<br>BRCHG).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

#### <span id="page-83-0"></span>**21.7.13.4.2.5 (10-01-2007)**

#### **Resolving Duplicate EINs**

<span id="page-83-1"></span>If, during the research process, you discover that an entity has been assigned two EINs, see IRM 21.7.13.6.3, Resolving Multiple EINs (CC BRCHG), for instructions on resolving this condition. (1)

### **21.7.13.4.2.6 (12-18-2015)**

### **Reactivating an EIN (TC 000)**

- Prior to January 1, 2008, an EIN that was assigned but not used within a three year period was dropped from Master File in an annual extract run at the end of each year. These EINs are not found using Command Codes ENMOD, BMFOL, or INOLE, but are still maintained on Command Codes NAMEE and NAMEB. (1)
- The IAT EIN Assignment tool accesses CC NAMEE/NAMEB and will locate these entities. (2)
- If an EIN is located using the IAT EIN Assignment tool, and you determine it belongs to the entity, the tool provides an option to reactivate the account. Continue to input information into the tool, and the tool will input the TC 000 to complete the reactivation. (3)
- If the tool is not available and an EIN is located by manually inputting CC NAMEE/NAMEB and you can determine it belongs to the entity, reactivate the account by first inputting CC ENMOD, then CC ENREQ as shown below. Take this action whether the inquiry is received on the phone or by correspondence. (4)

|      | Element        |                                                                               |
|------|----------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Line | Name           | Description<br>and<br>Validity                                                |
| 1    | ENREQ          | Command<br>Code—required                                                      |
| 1    | INTEND<br>TO   | TC000<br>INTEND<br>TO<br>BUILD<br>INDICATOR<br>—<br>"1"                       |
|      | BUILD          | must<br>be<br>entered<br>in<br>position<br>20<br>of<br>line<br>1<br>if<br>the |
|      | INDICATOR      | intent<br>is<br>to<br>establish<br>an<br>account<br>on<br>the<br>Master       |
|      |                | File<br>(a<br>TC<br>000<br>will<br>be<br>input).                              |
| 2    | NM-CTRL        | Name<br>Control<br>—<br>Must<br>meet<br>Standard<br>criteria                  |
|      |                | for<br>a<br>TIN<br>Name<br>Control                                            |
| 2    | CASE<br>STATUS | Case<br>Status<br>Code—"A"<br>or<br>"C"                                       |
| 2    | CASE<br>CTRL   | Case<br>Control<br>—<br>Must<br>be<br>a<br>valid<br>Case<br>Category          |
|      |                | Code.                                                                         |

| Line | Element<br>Name | Description<br>and<br>Validity                                              |
|------|-----------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 2    | IRS<br>RECEIVED | IRS<br>Received<br>Date<br>—<br>An<br>*<br>(asterisk)<br>in<br>the<br>first |
|      | DATE            | position<br>will<br>generate<br>current<br>date.                            |

The response to the above entries is a CC BNCHG screen pre-populated with the EIN and Name Control. Input **TC 000** and all information including Primary, Sort, and Care-of Name lines, X-Ref TIN or Sole Prop TIN, Location and Mailing Addresses, BOD, WPD, Employment Code, Filing Requirements etc. This information is to be gathered from a paper Form SS-4, or verbally from the taxpayer or their authorized third party representative. (5)

<span id="page-84-0"></span>**Note:** When reactivating accounts with no filing requirements ("O" files), input a "1" in the NOT-REQUIRED> field. Otherwise, an error message will be returned stating "AT LEAST ONE FIL REQ MUST BE INPUT" .

The TC 000 will post to Master File and re-establish the entity. Always send Notice Gatekeeper Web (SNIP) - LTR 0147C Detail Page (irs.gov) to the taxpayer. (6)

**Note:** If the taxpayer and/or their authorized representative requests an immediate fax confirmation of their EIN, fax accordingly.

#### <span id="page-84-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.2.7 (11-13-2018)**

#### **Taxpayer Claims They Did Not Request EIN**

Identity theft occurs when someone uses your name, SSN/TIN, credit card number or some other piece of your personal information. Some taxpayers have contacted EIN units after receiving a CP 575 identifying them as the owner of a new EIN. They claim they did not apply for an EIN. (1)

<span id="page-84-2"></span>**Reminder:** Before releasing any information or advising the taxpayer of actions to take, you must determine whether you are speaking to the taxpayer or to a third party acting on behalf of the taxpayer. Use guidance in IRM 21.1.3.2.3, Required Taxpayer Authentication.

Take action on a case by case basis. There is no specific order or process to follow. The main thing is to be sure the person did not apply and does not want the number associated with their name. Use the table below to assist you. (2)

**Reminder:** Most of the situations when a taxpayer contacts us stating they did not request an EIN are when a third party requested an EIN on the taxpayer's behalf for a legitimate business purpose. Therefore, it is important to determine if that is the situation which led to the taxpayer contacting us.

<span id="page-85-1"></span><span id="page-85-0"></span>

| If                                                                                    | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>A<br>taxpayer<br>indicates<br>that<br>they did<br>not<br>apply for<br>an<br>EIN | Determine<br>that<br>the<br>number<br>was<br>not<br>applied<br>for<br>by<br>a<br>spouse<br>or<br>other<br>family member,<br>a<br>neighborhood<br>club,<br>or<br>an<br>accountant<br>or<br>other<br>third<br>party<br>on<br>their<br>behalf<br>(such<br>as<br>a<br>fiscal<br>agent,<br>bank<br>or<br>executor<br>of<br>a<br>trust).<br>Note:<br>Thorough<br>research<br>and/or<br>direct<br>contact<br>with<br>the<br>customer<br>can<br>usually resolve<br>the<br>situation.<br>One<br>item<br>you<br>may want<br>to<br>determine<br>is<br>whether<br>both |
|                                                                                       | addresses<br>(the<br>one<br>on<br>the<br>notice<br>and<br>the<br>address<br>of<br>record)<br>are<br>the<br>same.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| 2)<br>The<br>addresses<br>are<br>the<br>same                                          | Probe<br>further<br>on<br>the<br>above<br>issues.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| 3)<br>The                                                                             | Determine<br>if<br>customer<br>is<br>aware<br>of<br>the<br>other<br>address.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| addresses<br>are<br>different                                                         | Reminder:<br>The<br>CP<br>575<br>is<br>issued<br>to<br>the<br>address<br>on<br>lines<br>4/5<br>on<br>Form<br>SS-4.<br>Therefore,<br>if<br>a<br>third<br>party<br>designee<br>submitted<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>with<br>the<br>taxpayer's<br>address,<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>would<br>receive<br>the<br>CP<br>575<br>and<br>may not<br>be<br>aware<br>that<br>the<br>third<br>party submitted<br>the<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>on<br>the<br>taxpayer's<br>behalf.<br>The<br>third<br>party<br>does<br>not<br>receive<br>the<br>CP<br>575.                                |
| 4)<br>The<br>taxpayer<br>believes<br>their<br>identity has<br>been<br>stolen          | Follow<br>guidance<br>in<br>25.23.11.4,<br>Business<br>Master<br>File<br>(BMF)<br>ID<br>Theft<br>Research.<br>Each<br>BMF<br>site<br>has<br>a<br>specific<br>group<br>handling<br>BMF<br>Identity theft<br>inquires.<br>Referral<br>procedures<br>are<br>found<br>in<br>IRM<br>25.23.11.6.4,<br>BMF<br>Identify Theft<br>Paper<br>Inquiry,<br>and<br>IRM<br>25.23.11.6.5,<br>BMF<br>Identify Theft<br>Inquiry Made<br>to<br>a<br>BMF<br>AM<br>CSR.                                                                                                         |

#### <span id="page-85-2"></span>**21.7.13.4.3 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Entity Classification and Ownership Changes**

If an EIN request is received indicating a change in ownership, examine the request carefully to determine whether a new entity has been created or only the name has been changed. (1)

- This subsection contains information to help you determine whether an EIN is needed when an entity changes its classification or ownership changes to the following entities: (2)
  - Sole Proprietorships
  - Corporations
  - Partnerships
  - Disregarded Entities
- <span id="page-86-0"></span>See IRM 3.13.2, BMF Account Numbers, for more information on rules concerning Form 8832, Entity Classification Election, and Form 2553, Election by a Small Business Corporation. (3)

**Note:** During EIN assignment, ensure the correct filing requirements for the entity being established will be assigned, regardless of notations on the Form SS-4 or statements from the taxpayer that Form 8832 or Form 2553 will subsequently be filed with the IRS. On the phone, explain to the taxpayer that once the Form 8832 and/or Form 2553 have been processed, the account will be updated to reflect the entity classification change. Do not correspond with the taxpayer on this issue, as the CP 575 discusses entity classification changes.

### <span id="page-86-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.3.1 (10-01-2007)**

#### **Entity Classification Changes Requiring a New EIN**

The table below identifies entity type changes that require issuance of a new EIN. (1)

| From                          | To                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|-------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Individual/Sole<br>Proprietor | Partnership<br>Corporation                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|                               | Exceptions:<br>A<br>new<br>EIN<br>is<br>not<br>necessary if:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|                               | An<br>individual<br>is<br>doing<br>business<br>as<br>a<br>Limited<br>Liability Company and<br>changes<br>its<br>classification<br>by filing<br>Form<br>8832,<br>Entity<br>Classification,<br>or<br>A<br>disregarded<br>entity changes<br>its<br>classification,<br>so<br>it<br>is<br>recognized<br>as<br>a<br>separate<br>entity,<br>and<br>the<br>entity already has<br>an<br>EIN. |
|                               | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.1.3,<br>Sole<br>Proprietor<br>Attempting<br>to<br>File<br>as<br>a<br>Corporation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Partnership                   | Individual/Sole<br>Proprietor<br>or<br>Corporation                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Corporation                   | Individual/Sole<br>Proprietor<br>Partnership                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |

**Note:** See IRM 3.13.2.26, Domestic Limited Liability Company (LLC), for information on entity classification changes involving LLCs.

#### <span id="page-87-0"></span>**21.7.13.4.3.2 (01-13-2009)**

#### **Changes to Sole Proprietorships**

- Assign a new EIN to a sole proprietorship if any of the following are true: (1)
  - The sole proprietorship changes ownership from one individual to another.
  - The sole proprietor goes into bankruptcy (except under IRC Chapter 12 or 13). Assign a new EIN to the Bankruptcy Estate. Do not assign another sole proprietor EIN to the taxpayer.
  - The sole proprietor dies, and either an estate or a spouse (when there is no estate involved) takes over the business.

<span id="page-87-1"></span>**Note:** If the decedent and spouse have been filing a joint return for household employment taxes only, and the spouse takes over as employer, a new EIN is required for the spouse after the first year of the ownership change.

- The sole proprietor takes in partners and operates as a partnership.
- The sole proprietor incorporates.
- Do not assign a new EIN to a sole proprietorship under the following circumstances: (2)
  - The sole proprietor has one business and opens a second sole proprietorship. (An individual is permitted to have only one identification number regardless of the number or types of sole proprietorships they operate.)

#### <span id="page-88-0"></span>**21.7.13.4.3.3 (10-01-2008)**

### **Changes to Corporations**

- Assign a new EIN to a corporation if any of the following are true: (1)
  - A corporation is operating under a new corporate charter.
  - A new corporation is created after a statutory merger.
- Do not assign a new EIN to a corporation under the following circumstances: (2)
  - The corporation changes its name only, the structure of the corporation remains unchanged, and it operates under the same charter.
  - The corporation files bankruptcy.
  - The corporation purchases another employing entity, a consolidated return is filed, and the purchaser uses the original EIN.
  - The entity changes its classification by filing Form 8832, Entity Classification.

#### <span id="page-88-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.3.4 (10-01-2019)**

#### **Changes to Partnerships**

Assign a new EIN to a partnership when the partnership terminates (all of its operations are discontinued and no part of any business, financial (1)

operation, or venture is continued by any of its partners in a partnership) and a new partnership is begun.

- A new EIN is not necessary if any of the following are true: (2)
  - The partnership terminates because of a sale or exchange of more than 50 percent of the total interests in the partnership capital and profits (See Treas. Reg 1.708-1(b)(4), example (ii), referencing 301.6109-1(d)(2)(iii) indicating the new partnership retains the EIN of the terminated partnership.) IRC 708(b)(1)(B).

<span id="page-89-0"></span>**Note:** Section 708(b)(1)(B) was repealed by the TCJA, effective for tax years beginning after December 31, 2017.

- The entity changes its classification by filing Form 8832, Entity Classification.
- The partnership declares bankruptcy.
- The partnership changes locations or adds locations.
- The partnership changes its name.

### **21.7.13.4.3.5 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Disregarded Entities**

- A disregarded entity is a business entity having a single owner, which can be an individual or another business entity. If the entity is disregarded for income tax purposes, its activities are treated as a sole proprietorship (if the owner is an individual), or as a branch or division of the owning entity (if the owner is a business entity). Generally, the taxpayer will inform you that they are a disregarded entity. As of January 1, 2009, single member LLCs that are not taxed as corporations are treated as separate from their owners for employment tax purposes. (1)
- Assign an EIN to a single member LLC not taxed as a corporation, if the entity does not already have an EIN and: (2)
  - The entity has employees for the first time and the owner needs to obtain an EIN for employment tax reporting purposes, or
  - The owner wants to obtain an EIN for purposes other than federal tax reporting.

#### <span id="page-89-1"></span>**21.7.13.4.4 (05-25-2012)**

### **EINs Required for Business Purposes**

<span id="page-90-0"></span>If a taxpayer indicates that an EIN is needed for business purposes (e.g., to acquire professional licenses, to collect sales tax on retail sales, or for banking purposes), then assign an EIN, unless the entity already has one. (1)

**Caution:** A responsible party may only receive one (1) EIN per day. See IRM 21.7.13.2.2.2, How Many EINs a Responsible Party Can Receive Each Day, for more information.

#### <span id="page-90-1"></span>**21.7.13.5 (11-18-2024)**

### **Assigning EINs**

- Accounts Management employees are required to use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool when assigning EINs. (1)
- ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ ≡ (2)
- <span id="page-90-2"></span>(3) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs.

#### **21.7.13.5.1 (03-02-2018)**

#### **EIN Assignment: Sole Proprietorship**

This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for sole proprietorships. (1)

#### **21.7.13.5.1.1 (10-01-2024)**

### **Definition: Sole Proprietorship**

- A sole proprietorship is an unincorporated business that is owned by one individual. It is the simplest form of business organization to start and maintain. (1)
  - The business has no existence apart from the owner.
  - Its liabilities are all personal liabilities and the owner undertakes the risks of the business for all assets owned, whether or not used in the business.

<span id="page-90-3"></span>**Note:** For more information on sole proprietorships, see Publication 334, Tax Guide for Small Businesses. Information for farmers can be found in Publication 225, Farmer's Tax Guide.

Spouses would **not** be considered a sole proprietorship, even if they are located in a Community Property state. (2)

#### <span id="page-91-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.1.2 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Sole Proprietorship**

- Established EINs can only be disclosed to: (1)
  - The individual or
  - Third party authorized by the individual
- Before disclosing an EIN to a third party, make sure you have a valid Form 2848, Power of Attorney and Declaration of Representative, Form 8821, Tax Information Authorization, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, (1) Step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)
- If authorization is not available, inform the third party requesting the EIN that you are going to: (3)
  - Take the information from the taxpayer and assign an EIN, and
  - Send notification (CP 575) of the EIN to the taxpayer's address of record.

<span id="page-91-1"></span>**Note:** If a previously assigned EIN is located, do not disclose this fact to an unauthorized third party.

### **21.7.13.5.1.3 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Sole Proprietor Attempting to File as a Corporation**

- A sole proprietor cannot file a corporate tax return, unless they are doing business through an eligible business, such as a Limited Liability Company (LLC). (1)
- If there is an indication that the taxpayer is changing from a sole proprietorship to a corporation, advise the taxpayer that they must obtain a new EIN. (2)
- <span id="page-91-2"></span>If you receive Form 8832 with Form SS-4: (3)
  - a. Assign the EIN.

**Note:** Do not assign 1120 filing requirement.

- b. Notate the EIN on Form 8832.
- c. Forward the forms daily to the correct BMF Entity team. See IRM 21.7.13.7.2.2, Cases Forwarded to Submission Processing BMF Entity.
- d. Include a request that the Forms 8832 be processed on an expedited basis.

<span id="page-92-0"></span>**Note:** After a classification has been elected, it cannot change for the next five years without a private letter ruling.

#### <span id="page-92-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.1.4 (10-01-2024)**

#### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Sole Proprietor**

- Assign an EIN if a legitimate reason exists for the EIN, such as the individual: (1)
  - Is the administrator of a pension plan
  - Is doing business with a federal agency (that is, contracting)
  - Is classified as an independent contractor and has, or plans to have employees
  - Is classified as an independent contractor and is liable for employment or excise tax
  - Is establishing a pension, profit sharing, or retirement plan
  - Is planning to have employees or is liable for employment or excise tax
  - Has household employees
  - Indicates that the EIN is required for business purposes
  - Is concerned about Identity Theft and wishes to use an EIN instead of their Social Security Number for business purposes **Exception:** Individual Retirement Account (IRA) trusts do not require an EIN unless the trust has to file Form 990-T or Form 1041.

<span id="page-92-3"></span><span id="page-92-2"></span>**Note:** A sole proprietor, who has not previously applied for an EIN, may attempt to open a retirement account, such as a Keogh, which is available to self-employed persons. The bank or financial institution will advise the taxpayer they must have an EIN to do this. The taxpayer may then think they are applying for a 401K or IRA EIN, when in fact, all they need is a sole proprietor EIN. Be alert to this situation and explain to the taxpayer that you will be assigning them an EIN as a sole proprietor and they should use this EIN for all their sole proprietor business needs, including opening retirement accounts available to self-employed persons.

- Assigning an EIN for the sole reason of improving or restoring an individual's credit or for obtaining a loan is not a legal business purpose. (2)
- Follow the criteria in the table below when individual ownership changes within the same year. (3)

<span id="page-93-0"></span>

| If                               | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|----------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>An<br>individual's         | Correspond<br>to<br>inform<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>that<br>they                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| spouse<br>is<br>added<br>to      | are<br>required<br>to<br>file<br>as<br>a<br>partnership.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| indicate<br>part                 | Note:<br>Assign<br>a<br>new<br>EIN<br>since<br>it<br>is<br>a<br>different                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| ownership<br>in<br>the           | entity type.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| business                         | Caution:<br>Taxpayers<br>may be<br>attempting<br>to<br>follow<br>IRC<br>761<br>(f)<br>which<br>provides<br>that<br>for<br>tax<br>years<br>beginning<br>after<br>12/31/2006,<br>a<br>qualified<br>joint<br>venture<br>conducted<br>by both<br>spouses<br>who<br>file<br>a<br>joint<br>return<br>is<br>not<br>rated<br>as<br>a<br>partnership<br>for<br>federal<br>tax<br>purposes.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.3.1,<br>Definition:<br>Partnerships,<br>paragraph<br>(3)<br>for<br>information<br>and<br>instructions. |
| 2)<br>A<br>spouse<br>is          | Assign<br>a<br>new<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| dropped<br>from<br>the           |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| entity (change<br>from           |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| partnership<br>to<br>sole        |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| proprietorship)                  |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 3)<br>An<br>individual           | Only one<br>EIN<br>is<br>needed.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| operates<br>more<br>than         |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| one<br>business                  |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 4)<br>An<br>individual<br>has    | Only one<br>EIN<br>is<br>needed.<br>The<br>EIN<br>can<br>be<br>used                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| both<br>regular                  | for<br>both<br>the<br>business<br>and<br>household                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| employees<br>and                 | employees<br>to<br>withhold,<br>report<br>and<br>pay                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| household<br>employees           | employment<br>taxes<br>on<br>Form<br>941<br>or<br>Form<br>944,                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|                                  | Form<br>940<br>or<br>Form<br>1040,<br>Schedule<br>H.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

| the<br>individual<br>stays<br>in | retains<br>their<br>original<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

#### <span id="page-93-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.1.5 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Before Assigning EIN: Sole Proprietor**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |  |
|------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 1    | Validate<br>the<br>taxpayer's<br>SSN<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |  |
|      | CC<br>INOLE<br>CC<br>NAMEI,<br>and                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMES<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                                                                  |  |
| 2    | Research<br>the<br>sole<br>proprietor's<br>name<br>and<br>trade<br>name<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                                                     |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB,<br>and<br>CC<br>NAMEE                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |  |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |  |
|      | Examples:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB:<br>Falcon,John<br>(name)<br>or<br>Falcon<br>Plumbing,+,<br>(trade)                                                                                                                                                                                                       |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEE:<br>John]Falcon<br>(name),<br>or<br>Falcon<br>John                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |  |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |  |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number<br>by<br>researching<br>it<br>on<br>ENMOD<br>and<br>INOLES.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>CC<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN. |  |
