#### <span id="page-98-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.2 (03-02-2018)**

### <span id="page-98-1"></span>**EIN Assignment: Corporation**

(1) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for corporations.

### **21.7.13.5.2.1 (10-01-2013)**

#### **Definition: Corporation**

- A corporation is defined as a legal entity or structure created under the authority of the laws of a state consisting of a person or group of persons who become shareholders. The entity's existence is considered separate and distinct from that of its shareholders. Since a corporation is an entity in its own right, it is liable for its own debts and obligations. In forming a corporation, prospective shareholders transfer money, property, or both, for the corporation's capital stock. (1)
- A personal service corporation is an organization in which: (2)
  - The activity involves the performance of services in the field of Health, Law, Engineering, Architecture, Accounting, Actuarial Science, Performing Arts, or Consulting, and
  - Substantially all of the stock is owned by the employees who perform the services.
- The table below describes the associated terms and guidelines for a corporation. (3)

<span id="page-99-1"></span><span id="page-99-0"></span>

| Term                | Guidelines                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |  |
|---------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| Subsidiary          | A<br>subsidiary of<br>a<br>corporation:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |  |
|                     | Must<br>have<br>its<br>own<br>EIN<br>Files<br>a<br>separate<br>charter<br>with<br>the<br>Secretary<br>of<br>State<br>Issues<br>its<br>own<br>stock,<br>and<br>Files<br>its<br>own<br>employment<br>tax<br>returns,<br>but<br>has<br>the<br>option<br>to<br>file<br>Form<br>1120<br>with<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation<br>or<br>on<br>its<br>own<br>Note:<br>The<br>subsidiary must<br>have<br>the<br>same<br>tax<br>year                                                                                 |  |
|                     | as<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation<br>if<br>the<br>subsidiary<br>is<br>filing<br>a<br>consolidated<br>return<br>with<br>the<br>parent.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |  |
| Division            | A<br>division<br>of<br>a<br>corporation:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |  |
|                     | Is<br>an<br>extension<br>of<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation;<br>it<br>is<br>not<br>a<br>separate<br>entity,<br>and<br>Can<br>make<br>Federal<br>Tax<br>Deposit<br>(FTD)<br>payments<br>but<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation's<br>name,<br>address,<br>EIN,<br>etc.<br>must<br>be<br>maintained                                                                                                                                                                                                              |  |
|                     | The<br>parent<br>corporation<br>consolidates<br>the<br>tax<br>information<br>of<br>a<br>division<br>with<br>its<br>return.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |  |
| Corporate<br>Merger | A<br>corporate<br>merger<br>occurs<br>when<br>one<br>corporation<br>acquires<br>the<br>assets<br>and<br>liabilities<br>of<br>another<br>corporation<br>and<br>the<br>two<br>combine<br>under<br>applicable<br>law<br>to<br>form<br>one<br>corporation.<br>The<br>corporation<br>that<br>does<br>not<br>survive<br>must<br>submit<br>the<br>applicable<br>final<br>returns<br>to<br>close<br>out<br>its<br>account.<br>The<br>surviving<br>corporation<br>continues<br>to<br>use<br>its<br>original<br>EIN. |  |
| Affiliate           | Each<br>affiliated<br>corporation:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |  |
|                     | Has<br>its<br>own<br>charter,<br>and<br>Can<br>have<br>a<br>different<br>tax<br>year<br>from<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |  |
|                     | Note:<br>If<br>the<br>affiliate<br>files<br>a<br>consolidated<br>return<br>with<br>the<br>parent<br>company,<br>it<br>must<br>have<br>the<br>same<br>tax<br>year.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |  |

### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Corporation**

- Established EINs can only be disclosed to individuals who can legally bind the corporation. The authority to bind means the ability to execute agreements that are binding and legally enforceable against the corporation under state law. Individuals who can legally bind the corporation frequently include: (1)
  - President
  - Vice president
  - Corporate secretary
  - Corporate treasurer
  - Chief executive officer

<span id="page-100-0"></span>**Caution:** A corporate officer, who is not the president of a corporation, must be asked if they can legally bind the corporation.

- EINs cannot be disclosed to a personal secretary or assistant unless they can legally bind the corporation. Request one of the following documents in this case: (2)
  - Articles of incorporation stating that they are legally authorized to bind the corporation, or
  - Correspondence on corporation letterhead, signed by the president of the corporation, stating that they are authorized to bind the corporation.
- EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid: (3)
  - Form 2848, Power of Attorney (POA)
  - Form 8821, Taxpayer Information Authorization (TIA), or
  - A taxpayer signed Third Party Designee authorization on the Form SS-4

<span id="page-100-1"></span>**Note:** See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, (1) step 7 for more information on third party disclosure.

<span id="page-100-2"></span>If the corporation is incorporated in Delaware, then the incorporator is allowed to receive the EIN. (4)

### **21.7.13.5.2.3 (10-01-2006)**

**Determining the Need for an EIN: Corporation**

Use the information in the table below to determine the need for an EIN for a corporation. (1)

<span id="page-101-0"></span>

| If |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Then<br>a<br>new<br>EIN<br>is |
|----|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| 1) |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Needed.                       |
|    | The<br>entity became<br>a<br>new<br>subsidiary of<br>a<br>corporation<br>The<br>entity is<br>a<br>subsidiary of<br>a<br>corporation<br>and<br>currently uses<br>the<br>parent<br>corporation's<br>EIN<br>The<br>corporation<br>becomes<br>a<br>partnership<br>or<br>sole<br>proprietorship<br>A<br>corporation<br>went<br>out<br>of<br>business<br>and<br>reopened<br>with<br>a<br>new<br>charter<br>A<br>bank<br>foreclosed<br>on<br>a<br>corporation<br>and<br>kept<br>the<br>business<br>open<br>with<br>the<br>bank<br>as<br>the<br>taxpaying<br>entity<br>Note:<br>In<br>the<br>case<br>of<br>a<br>bank<br>foreclosure,<br>set<br>up<br>the<br>account<br>with<br>the<br>bank<br>as<br>the<br>taxpaying<br>entity<br>and<br>the<br>business<br>name<br>as<br>the<br>DBA.  |                               |
| 2) | The<br>entity is<br>a<br>division<br>of<br>a<br>corporation<br>After<br>a<br>corporate<br>merger,<br>the<br>surviving<br>corporation<br>uses<br>its<br>existing<br>EIN<br>A<br>corporation<br>declares<br>bankruptcy<br>The<br>business<br>name<br>changes<br>The<br>location<br>changes<br>or<br>new<br>ones<br>are<br>added<br>(stores,<br>manufacturing<br>plants,<br>enterprises,<br>or<br>branches)<br>The<br>entity chooses<br>to<br>be<br>taxed<br>as<br>an<br>S<br>corporation<br>After<br>a<br>corporation<br>reorganization,<br>the<br>only<br>change<br>is<br>either<br>identity,<br>form,<br>or<br>place<br>of<br>organization<br>A<br>corporation<br>is<br>sold<br>and<br>the<br>assets,<br>liabilities,<br>and<br>charters<br>are<br>obtained<br>by the<br>buyer | Not<br>needed.                |

#### **21.7.13.5.2.4 (04-23-2019)**

**Research Before Assigning an EIN: Corporation**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

<span id="page-102-0"></span>

| Step | Action                                                                                             |  |  |  |
|------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|--|
| 1    | Verify the<br>responsible<br>party's<br>name<br>and<br>SSN,<br>ITIN<br>or<br>EIN<br>using          |  |  |  |
|      | CC<br>INOLE.<br>This<br>information<br>is<br>found<br>on<br>Lines<br>7a<br>and<br>7b<br>of<br>Form |  |  |  |
|      | SS-4.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                     |  |  |  |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.3.2.7,<br>Foreign<br>Entities<br>-<br>Definitions<br>and                     |  |  |  |
|      | Instructions,<br>for<br>important<br>information<br>on<br>foreign                                  |  |  |  |
|      | entities/persons.                                                                                  |  |  |  |
|      | Exception:<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>applications<br>(mailed/faxed)<br>with<br>a                          |  |  |  |
|      | received<br>date<br>of<br>May 13,<br>2019<br>and<br>subsequent<br>cannot<br>list<br>an             |  |  |  |
|      | entity (EIN)<br>as<br>the<br>responsible<br>party.<br>The<br>responsible<br>party                  |  |  |  |
|      | must<br>be<br>an<br>individual<br>with<br>a<br>valid<br>SSN/ITIN.                                  |  |  |  |
| 2    | Research<br>the<br>corporation's<br>name:                                                          |  |  |  |
|      |                                                                                                    |  |  |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB                                                                                        |  |  |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEE                                                                                        |  |  |  |
|      |                                                                                                    |  |  |  |
|      | Examples:                                                                                          |  |  |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB:<br>Falcon<br>&<br>Sons<br>Inc.,+,                                                     |  |  |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEE:<br>Falcon<br>&<br>Sons<br>Inc.                                                        |  |  |  |
|      |                                                                                                    |  |  |  |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                   |  |  |  |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM               |  |  |  |
|      | 21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.                                     |  |  |  |
|      | Note:<br>There<br>cannot<br>be<br>more<br>than<br>one<br>active<br>corporation                     |  |  |  |
|      | with<br>the<br>same<br>name<br>in<br>the<br>same<br>state.<br>If<br>the<br>taxpayer                |  |  |  |
|      | wishes<br>to<br>use<br>the<br>name<br>of<br>an<br>existing<br>entity,<br>obtain                    |  |  |  |
|      | documentation<br>from<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>verifying<br>that<br>the                               |  |  |  |
|      | name<br>is<br>registered<br>with<br>the<br>state.                                                  |  |  |  |
|      | If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                  |  |  |  |
|      |                                                                                                    |  |  |  |

#### <span id="page-102-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.2.5 (02-20-2013)**

**Determining Filing Requirement: Corporation**

Use the table below to determine the filing requirement for a corporation. (1)

<span id="page-103-0"></span>

| If<br>the<br>type<br>of<br>entity<br>indicated<br>is | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>A<br>for-profit<br>corporation                 | Enter<br>the<br>correct<br>Form<br>1120<br>filing<br>requirement<br>as<br>indicated<br>by the<br>nature<br>of<br>the<br>business.<br>If<br>you<br>cannot<br>determine<br>the<br>correct<br>1120<br>filing<br>requirement<br>based<br>on<br>the<br>nature<br>of<br>the<br>business,<br>enter<br>1120–01.<br>Note:<br>On<br>a<br>phone<br>call,<br>ask<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>what<br>type<br>of<br>Form<br>1120<br>they will<br>be<br>filing.<br>If<br>the<br>caller<br>is<br>unsure,<br>enter<br>1120–01.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.5.2,<br>Tax<br>Form<br>and<br>Filing<br>Requirement<br>Descriptions<br>for<br>Corporations,<br>for<br>more<br>information<br>about<br>corporate<br>filing<br>requirements. |

| If<br>the<br>type<br>of<br>entity                                                                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| indicated<br>is                                                                                                                                                                                    | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 2)<br>An<br>S<br>corporation<br>(Sub<br>chapter<br>S<br>or<br>Sub<br>S)                                                                                                                            | On<br>a<br>phone<br>call,<br>advise<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>to<br>obtain<br>Form<br>2553<br>and<br>instructions<br>from<br>IRS.gov ,<br>or<br>call<br>800-829-3676<br>and<br>request<br>the<br>form<br>and<br>instructions<br>by mail.<br>For<br>paper<br>and<br>fax<br>applications,<br>the<br>CP<br>575<br>notice<br>instructs<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>to<br>file<br>Form<br>2553.<br>Taxpayers<br>who<br>apply over<br>the<br>internet<br>are<br>provided<br>with<br>this<br>information<br>during<br>the<br>online<br>session.<br>Do<br>not<br>establish<br>the<br>filing<br>requirement<br>of<br>1120–02<br>during<br>EIN<br>assignment.<br>If<br>Form<br>2553<br>is<br>attached:<br>Notate<br>the<br>EIN<br>on<br>the<br>Form<br>2553. |
|                                                                                                                                                                                                    | Route<br>to<br>the<br>correct<br>BMF<br>Entity<br>Team.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.2.2,<br>Cases<br>Forwarded<br>to<br>Submission<br>Processing<br>BMF<br>Entity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| 3)<br>Incorporated<br>in<br>the                                                                                                                                                                    | The<br>entity must<br>file<br>Form<br>1120.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| United<br>States                                                                                                                                                                                   | Note:<br>This<br>includes<br>all<br>U.S.<br>Territories<br>except<br>Puerto<br>Rico.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| 4)<br>A<br>foreign<br>company,<br>and<br>is<br>not<br>incorporated<br>in<br>the<br>U.S.<br>but<br>does<br>business<br>in<br>the<br>U.S.<br>or<br>has<br>a<br>branch<br>office<br>in<br>the<br>U.S. | The<br>entity must<br>file<br>Form<br>1120-F,<br>Income<br>Tax<br>Return<br>of<br>a<br>Foreign<br>Corporation<br>Input<br>a<br>filing<br>requirement<br>of<br>06.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |

<span id="page-104-0"></span>Organizations of professional persons organized under State Professional Association Acts are treated as a corporation for tax purposes. (2)

<span id="page-105-0"></span>For a Personal Service Corporation, input a Form 1120 filing requirement of **19**. The FYM must be 12. (3)

> **Note:** Form 1120 FRC of **19**cannot be input via CC BNCHG. If a Personal Service Corporation's filing requirement is incorrect, change it to Form 1120 FRC of 01. The tax return will then update the filing requirement to **19.**

### <span id="page-105-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.2.6 (10-01-2020)**

#### **CC ESIGN Input: Corporations**

The table below describes the fields and the entries for corporations. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3, CC ESIGN Input Screen, for general input instructions. (1)

<span id="page-105-2"></span>

| Field           | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                         |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Master-File-IND | The<br>Master<br>File<br>indicator<br>(MFI)<br>is<br>B.<br>However,<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>a |
|                 | non-profit<br>corporation<br>without<br>employees,<br>assign<br>MFI<br>of<br>O.            |
|                 | Note:<br>A<br>non-profit<br>entity may be<br>incorporated.<br>This                         |
|                 | is<br>the<br>case<br>if<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>checks<br>the<br>corporation<br>box          |
|                 | on<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>but<br>also<br>indicates<br>that<br>they<br>are<br>a<br>non          |
|                 | profit<br>organization<br>(IRC<br>501(c)<br>or<br>similar<br>statement).                   |
| Loc-Cd          | Input<br>the<br>valid<br>two-digit<br>EIN<br>prefix<br>for<br>the<br>campus.               |
|                 | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.2.4,<br>How<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Assigned.                          |
|                 | Note:<br>The<br>last<br>two<br>positions<br>of<br>the<br>field<br>display<br>the           |
|                 | Area<br>Office<br>Code<br>(00).                                                            |

<span id="page-106-0"></span>

| Field     | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                       |
|-----------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Name-Ctrl | The<br>Name<br>Control<br>is<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>significant                      |
|           | characters<br>of<br>the<br>corporation's<br>name.                                        |
|           | Disregard<br>the<br>word<br>"the"<br>when<br>followed<br>by                              |
|           | more<br>than<br>one<br>word.                                                             |
|           | Example:<br>The<br>Meadowlark<br>Co.                                                     |
|           | Name<br>Control<br>is<br>MEAD                                                            |
|           | ESIGN<br>input<br>is<br>MEAD                                                             |
|           | Include<br>the<br>word<br>the<br>when<br>it<br>is<br>followed<br>by<br>only one<br>word. |
|           | Example:<br>The<br>Flamingo                                                              |
|           | Name<br>Control<br>is<br>THEF                                                            |
|           | ESIGN<br>input<br>is<br>THEF                                                             |
|           |                                                                                          |
|           | Use<br>corporate<br>Name<br>Control<br>rules<br>if<br>an                                 |
|           | individual<br>name<br>contains<br>the<br>following                                       |
|           | abbreviations:                                                                           |
|           | Example:                                                                                 |
|           | -PC<br>-<br>Professional<br>Corporation                                                  |
|           | -PA<br>-<br>Professional<br>Association                                                  |
|           | -SC<br>-<br>Small<br>Corporation,<br>or                                                  |
|           | -PS<br>-<br>Professional<br>Service                                                      |
|           |                                                                                          |
|           | Example:<br>John<br>Waxwing<br>PA                                                        |
|           | Use<br>corporate<br>Name<br>Control<br>rules<br>if<br>the                                |
|           | organization's<br>name<br>contains<br>the<br>words<br>Fund                               |
|           | or<br>Foundation.                                                                        |
|           | Example:<br>Kathryn<br>Canary Memorial<br>Fund.                                          |
|           | For<br>more<br>information<br>on<br>inputting<br>Name<br>Control,                        |
|           | see<br>Document<br>7071-A,<br>Name<br>Control<br>Job<br>Aid<br>-<br>For                  |
|           | Use<br>Outside<br>of<br>the<br>Entity Area.                                              |
|           |                                                                                          |

<span id="page-107-0"></span>

| Field                                      | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|--------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Primary-Name<br>Continuation<br>of-Primary | The<br>Primary Name<br>is<br>the<br>name<br>of<br>the<br>corporation<br>as<br>it<br>appears<br>on<br>the<br>state<br>charter.<br>Important:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Name                                       | Delete<br>the<br>word<br>"the"<br>unless<br>it<br>is<br>followed<br>by<br>only one<br>word.<br>Otherwise,<br>do<br>not<br>modify the<br>corporate<br>name.<br>Do<br>not<br>abbreviate,<br>change<br>symbols,<br>or<br>change<br>and<br>to<br>&.<br>The<br>ampersand<br>(&)<br>and<br>the<br>hyphen<br>(-)<br>are<br>considered<br>valid<br>characters<br>in<br>the<br>Primary<br>Name<br>line.<br>Suffixes<br>such<br>as<br>PA,<br>PC,<br>and<br>Inc.<br>indicate<br>a<br>corporate<br>entity and<br>must<br>be<br>input<br>with<br>the<br>corporation's<br>name.<br>Note:<br>Do<br>not<br>reject<br>a<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>if<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>did<br>not<br>include<br>a<br>corporate<br>ending<br>in<br>the<br>primary name<br>such<br>as<br>Co,<br>Inc,<br>PC<br>etc. |
| Sort-Name                                  | The<br>Sort<br>Name<br>is<br>the<br>trade<br>or<br>business<br>name<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>different<br>from<br>the<br>true<br>name.<br>The<br>Sort<br>Name<br>is<br>never                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|                                            | another<br>corporation<br>or<br>limited<br>liability<br>company (LLC)<br>name,<br>or<br>a<br>corporate<br>officer's<br>name<br>(president,<br>vice<br>president,<br>etc.).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|                                            | When<br>a<br>corporation<br>is<br>in<br>bankruptcy,<br>or<br>a<br>fiduciary<br>is<br>appointed<br>in<br>a<br>state<br>insolvency proceeding,<br>change<br>or<br>add<br>a<br>Sort<br>Name<br>to<br>show<br>the<br>receiver's,<br>trustee's<br>or<br>debtor<br>in<br>possession's<br>name.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Care-of-Name                               | (If<br>provided)<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.5,<br>Care<br>of<br>Name<br>Input,<br>for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| Mail-Street-Or<br>Foreign<br>City/Zip      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.2,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>Cit/Zip<br>Field,<br>for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |

<span id="page-108-0"></span>

| Field          | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                             |
|----------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Mail           | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.3,<br>Mail<br>City/State/ZIP<br>or<br>Foreign      |

| Country        |                                                                                |

| City/State/Zip | for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                  |
| Filing         | Entities<br>that<br>are<br>incorporated<br>with<br>a<br>state<br>are<br>also   |
| Requirement    | incorporated<br>for<br>federal<br>tax<br>purposes<br>except<br>that<br>a       |
|                | single<br>member<br>entity may be<br>incorporated<br>for<br>state              |
|                | purposes<br>but<br>disregarded<br>for<br>federal<br>income<br>tax              |
|                | purposes.<br>When<br>an<br>entity,<br>other<br>than<br>a<br>disregarded        |
|                | entity,<br>is<br>incorporated,<br>it<br>must<br>file<br>the<br>correct<br>Form |
|                | 1120,<br>unless<br>it<br>is<br>an<br>exempt<br>organization.<br>See<br>IRM     |
|                | 21.7.13.7.5.2,<br>Tax<br>Form<br>and<br>Filing<br>Requirement                  |

|                | Most<br>exempt<br>organizations<br>that<br>are<br>incorporated                 |

|                | those<br>affiliated<br>with<br>a<br>church<br>or<br>a<br>governmental          |

|                | by AM<br>EIN<br>Assistors.                                                     |

|                | Requirement<br>Input.                                                          |

<span id="page-109-0"></span>

| Field         | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|---------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| FYM           | The<br>Fiscal<br>Year<br>Month<br>(FYM)<br>is<br>the<br>month<br>in<br>which<br>the<br>fiscal<br>year<br>ends<br>for<br>the<br>corporation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|               | Corporations<br>can<br>determine<br>their<br>FYM,<br>unless<br>they are<br>a<br>small<br>business<br>corporation,<br>insurance<br>company,<br>or<br>a<br>personal<br>service<br>corporation.<br>These<br>company types<br>must<br>use<br>a<br>calendar<br>year<br>for<br>the<br>fiscal<br>year<br>(December<br>31).<br>The<br>taxpayer<br>is<br>responsible<br>for<br>determining<br>if<br>the<br>company is<br>a<br>small<br>business<br>corporation,<br>insurance<br>company,<br>or<br>a<br>personal<br>service<br>corporation.<br>If<br>the<br>FYM<br>is<br>blank<br>and<br>the<br>corporation<br>type<br>is<br>not<br>a<br>small<br>business<br>corporation,<br>insurance<br>company,<br>or<br>a<br>personal<br>service<br>corporation,<br>enter<br>the<br>month<br>preceding<br>the<br>business<br>operation<br>date<br>(BOD).<br>Once<br>a<br>FYM<br>is<br>determined<br>(return<br>filed),<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>can<br>only change<br>it<br>if<br>they meet |
|               | specific<br>criteria,<br>or<br>by filing<br>Form<br>1128.<br>For<br>information<br>on<br>the<br>specific<br>criteria<br>needed<br>for<br>changing<br>a<br>FYM,<br>see<br>IRM<br>3.13.2.21,<br>Form<br>1128<br>-<br>Application<br>to<br>Adopt,<br>Change<br>or<br>Retain<br>a<br>Tax<br>Year.<br>Caution:<br>Never<br>change<br>the<br>FYM<br>for<br>an<br>entity on<br>the<br>BMF,<br>unless<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>has<br>explained<br>the<br>reason<br>for<br>the<br>change<br>and<br>it<br>is<br>permissible<br>by law.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| XREF-TIN-Type | The<br>cross<br>reference<br>TIN<br>type<br>is<br>used<br>to<br>identify<br>if<br>the<br>number<br>is<br>an<br>EIN<br>or<br>a<br>SSN/ITIN.<br>Enter<br>the<br>number:<br>0<br>for<br>SSN/ITIN,<br>or<br>2<br>for<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|               | Exception:<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>applications<br>(mailed/faxed)<br>with<br>a<br>received<br>date<br>of<br>May 13,<br>2019<br>and<br>subsequent<br>cannot<br>list<br>an<br>entity (EIN)<br>as<br>the<br>responsible<br>party.<br>The<br>responsible<br>party must<br>be<br>an<br>individual<br>with<br>a<br>valid<br>SSN/ITIN.<br>Therefore<br>the<br>X-REF-TIN-Type<br>will<br>be<br>0.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

<span id="page-110-0"></span>

#### <span id="page-111-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.3 (03-02-2018)**

#### **EIN Assignment: Partnerships**

(1) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for partnerships.

#### **21.7.13.5.3.1 (10-01-2024)**

#### **Definition: Partnerships**

<span id="page-111-1"></span>A partnership includes a syndicate, group, pool, joint venture or other unincorporated organization, through or by means of which a business, financial operation, or venture is carried on, and which is not a trust, estate or corporation. (1)

**Note:** Individuals, corporations, trusts, estates, limited liability companies (LLC) and partnerships can be partners within a partnership.

<span id="page-111-2"></span>A domestic LLC with at least two members that does not file Form 8832 electing to be classified as an association taxable as a corporation is classified as a partnership for federal income tax purposes. (2)

**Note:** If an eligible entity has two members under local law, but one of the members is a disregarded entity owned by the other member, the

- entity cannot be classified as a partnership and is either taxed as a disregarded entity or can elect to be taxed as a corporation.
- Public Law 110-28, Small Business and Work Opportunity Tax Act of 2007, Section 8215 provides that for tax years beginning after 12/31/2006, a "qualified joint venture" conducted by spouses who file a joint return would not be treated as a partnership for federal tax purposes. **This is not a new entity type**. The law simply allows that the spouses are the sole owners of the joint venture, both materially participate in the trade or business, and file a joint individual tax return, they can elect to be treated as a "Qualified Joint Venture" . Each spouse must claim income and expenses on a separate Schedule C or F as sole proprietors. For tax purposes, these spouses are treated as sole proprietors. If the spouses need, or otherwise request EINs, each spouse should apply for one as a sole proprietor. (3)
- The table below describes the associated terms for a partnership. (4)

<span id="page-112-1"></span><span id="page-112-0"></span>

| Term                       | Description                                                                      |
|----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Partnership                | A<br>partnership<br>agreement<br>is<br>a<br>verbal<br>or<br>written              |
| Agreement                  | agreement<br>whose<br>purpose<br>is<br>to<br>create<br>a                         |
|                            | partnership.<br>Separate<br>partnerships<br>mean<br>different                    |
|                            | partnership<br>agreements<br>and<br>require<br>separate<br>EINs.                 |
| Sale<br>or<br>Exchange     | The<br>phrase<br>"sale<br>or exchange<br>of<br>50<br>percent<br>or more          |
| of<br>50<br>Percent<br>or  | of<br>the<br>total<br>interest<br>in<br>partnerships"<br>is<br>used<br>to        |
| More<br>of<br>the<br>Total | determine<br>if<br>the<br>partnership<br>has<br>terminated.                      |
| Interest<br>in             | Note:<br>IRC<br>708(b)(1)(B)<br>states<br>that<br>a<br>partnership<br>is         |
| Partnerships               | considered<br>terminated<br>if<br>within<br>a<br>12<br>month<br>period           |
|                            | there<br>was<br>a<br>sale<br>or<br>exchange<br>of<br>50<br>percent<br>or<br>more |
|                            | of<br>the<br>total<br>interest<br>in<br>the<br>partnership's<br>capital<br>and   |
|                            | profits.<br>Treasury Regulations<br>1.708-1<br>(b)<br>(4)                        |
|                            | Example<br>(ii)<br>and<br>301.6109-1<br>(d)<br>(2)<br>(iii)<br>provide<br>that   |
|                            | a<br>new<br>partnership<br>that<br>is<br>formed<br>as<br>a<br>result<br>of<br>a  |
|                            | partnership<br>that<br>is<br>terminated<br>under<br>IRC<br>708(b)(1)             |
|                            | (B)<br>must<br>retain<br>the<br>EIN<br>of<br>the<br>terminated                   |
|                            | partnership.                                                                     |
|                            | Note:<br>Section<br>708(b)(1)(B)<br>was<br>repealed<br>by the                    |
|                            | TCJA,<br>effective<br>for<br>tax<br>years<br>beginning<br>after                  |
|                            | December<br>31,<br>2017.                                                         |

| Term            | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|-----------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Schedule<br>K-1 | The<br>partnership<br>uses<br>Schedule<br>K-1<br>to<br>report<br>each<br>partner's<br>share<br>of<br>the<br>partnership's<br>income,<br>credits,<br>deductions,<br>etc.<br>All<br>Partnerships<br>must<br>complete<br>Schedule<br>K<br>and<br>Schedules<br>K-1<br>and<br>attach<br>them<br>to<br>Form<br>1065.<br>Partners<br>should<br>keep<br>the<br>K-1<br>with<br>their<br>individual<br>tax<br>records. |

#### <span id="page-113-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.3.2 (10-01-2007)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Partnerships**

- Established EINs can be disclosed to: (1)
  - A responsible and duly authorized partner (including general and limited partners), or
  - An authorized third party.

**Note:** Tax returns and return information can only be released to individuals as outlined in IRM 11.3.2.4.2, Partnerships.

EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or a signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, (1) step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)

#### <span id="page-113-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.3.3 (10-01-2017)**

#### **Determining Filing Requirement: Partnerships**

- Form 1065, U.S. Return of Partnership Income is filed: (1)
  - To report the income, deductions, gains, losses, etc. from the operation of a partnership
  - By all domestic partnerships and all foreign partnerships that either engage in a trade or business effectively connected with the United States, or derive income from sources in the United States, and
  - By religious and apostolic organizations that are exempt from income tax under IRC Section 501(d).

Use the table below to determine the filing requirement for a partnership. (2)

| If                                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Then                                |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>The<br>entity type<br>is<br>a                                                                                                                                                                                      | Enter<br>a<br>Form<br>1065          |
| partnership<br>joint<br>venture                                                                                                                                                                                          | filing<br>requirement<br>of<br>1.   |
| Caution:<br>The<br>term<br>"joint<br>venture"<br>in<br>this<br>case<br>is<br>not<br>the<br>same<br>as<br>the<br>"qualified<br>joint<br>venture"<br>above.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.3.1,<br>Definition:<br>Partnerships |                                     |
| 2)<br>If<br>the<br>Other<br>box<br>on<br>Form<br>SS-4,<br>line<br>9a<br>is                                                                                                                                               | Establish<br>the<br>entity          |
| checked<br>and<br>indicates<br>it<br>is<br>a<br>tenancy<br>in                                                                                                                                                            | with<br>a<br>Form<br>1065<br>filing |
| common                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | requirement<br>of<br>1.             |

#### <span id="page-114-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.3.4 (10-01-2019)**

### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Partnerships**

(1) Use the table below to determine the need for an EIN for partnerships.

<span id="page-115-0"></span>

| If<br>any | of<br>the<br>following criteria<br>is<br>met                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Then<br>a<br>new<br>EIN<br>is |
|-----------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| 1)        |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Needed.                       |
|           | The<br>partnership<br>requests<br>an<br>EIN<br>and<br>does<br>not<br>already have<br>one<br>A<br>partnership<br>incorporates<br>One<br>partner<br>takes<br>over<br>and<br>operates<br>as<br>a<br>sole<br>proprietorship<br>A<br>partnership<br>ends<br>and<br>a<br>new<br>one<br>is<br>begun<br>Exception:<br>A<br>new<br>partnership<br>that<br>is<br>formed<br>as<br>a<br>result<br>of<br>the<br>termination<br>of<br>a<br>partnership<br>under<br>section<br>708(b)(1)(B)<br>(where<br>there<br>is<br>a<br>sale<br>or<br>exchange<br>of<br>50<br>percent<br>or<br>more<br>of<br>the<br>total<br>interest<br>in<br>partnership<br>capital<br>and<br>profits<br>within<br>a<br>12-month<br>period)<br>retains<br>the<br>EIN<br>of<br>the<br>terminated<br>partnership<br>and<br>does<br>not<br>require<br>a<br>new<br>EIN.<br>Note:<br>Section<br>708(b)(1)(B)<br>was<br>repealed<br>by the<br>TCJA,<br>effective<br>for<br>tax<br>years<br>beginning<br>after<br>December<br>31,<br>2017.<br>A<br>bankrupt<br>partnership<br>establishes<br>a<br>liquidating |                               |
|           | trust<br>that<br>is<br>a<br>separate<br>entity for<br>tax<br>purposes.<br>See<br>paragraph<br>(2)<br>below.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                               |
| 2)        | A<br>partnership<br>declares<br>bankruptcy<br>The<br>partnership<br>name<br>changes,<br>or<br>The<br>location<br>of<br>the<br>partnership<br>changes<br>or<br>locations<br>are<br>added                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Not<br>needed.                |

<span id="page-115-2"></span><span id="page-115-1"></span>A bankrupt partnership that establishes an escrow account, settlement fund, or similar fund to liquidate or distribute assets must obtain a new EIN for that entity. (2)

**Note:** Correspondence may be needed for bankrupt partnerships that establish an escrow account, settlement fund, or similar fund to liquidate or distribute assets.

#### <span id="page-115-3"></span>**21.7.13.5.3.5 (04-23-2019)**

**Research Before Assigning an EIN: Partnerships**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

# <span id="page-116-1"></span><span id="page-116-0"></span>**Step Action** 1 Validate the partner's SSN/ITIN using: CC INOLE CC NAMEI CC NAMES If the partner is an entity and not an individual, validate its EIN using: CC INOLE CC NAMEB CC NAMEE **Exception:** Form SS-4 applications (mailed/faxed) with a received date of May 13, 2019, and subsequent **cannot** list an entity (EIN) as the responsible party. The responsible party must be an individual with a valid SSN/ITIN. **Note:** See IRM 21.7.13.3.2.7, Foreign Entities - Definitions and Instructions, for important information on foreign entities/persons. 2 Research the partnership's name using: CC NAMEB, and CC NAMEE **Examples**: CC NAMEB: Gazelle and Giraffe,+, CC NAMEE: Gazelle and Giraffe Ptrs CC NAMEI: Giraffe, John **Note:** Use the partners' names and DBA when researching.

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |  |
|------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                                  |  |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>CC<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN. |  |

#### <span id="page-117-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.3.6 (04-23-2019)**

|                  | established<br>over<br>the<br>internet.                                          |  |

<span id="page-118-1"></span><span id="page-118-0"></span>

| Field                              | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |  |
