#### <span id="page-121-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.4 (03-02-2018)**

#### **EIN Assignment: Limited Liability Company (LLC)**

<span id="page-121-1"></span>This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for limited liability companies (LLCs). (1)

#### **21.7.13.5.4.1 (10-01-2019)**

### **Definition: LLC**

- <span id="page-121-2"></span>A limited liability company (LLC) is an entity organized under the laws of a state or foreign country that: (1)
  - Has the limited liability feature of the C corporation
  - Is formed by filing articles of organization with the individual state's Secretary of State office, and
  - Can have two or more members or a single member **Note:** For federal income tax purposes, an LLC is not recognized as an entity type, instead, a LLC may be treated as a partnership

or corporation, or be disregarded as an entity separate from its owner.

- A single-member domestic LLC that accepts the default classification of disregarded entity, and wants an EIN for filing employment tax returns or Form 5472 or for non-federal purposes, should: (2)
  - Check the Other box on Line 9a of Form SS-4, and
  - Write "Disregarded Entity" , "Disregarded Entity-Sole Proprietorship" , or **Foreign-owned U.S. disregarded entity - Form 5472** in the space provided on Line 9a.
- A multi-member domestic LLC, that accepts the default classification, should check the "partnership" box. A multi-member domestic LLC, that will be filing Form 8832 or Form 2553, should check the "corporation" box. (3)
- There cannot be more than one active LLC with the same name in the same state. If the taxpayer wishes to use the name of an existing entity, obtain documentation from the taxpayer verifying that the name is registered with the state. (4)

#### <span id="page-122-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.2 (10-01-2024)**

#### **Determining Tax Classification and Filing Requirements: LLC**

- For federal income tax purposes: (1)
  - An LLC can be taxed as a corporation, partnership, or be disregarded as an entity separate from its owner, and
  - The number or type of members and existing characteristics determines the correct filing requirement
- It is the taxpayer's responsibility to determine the correct entity classification. (2)
- Line 8 of Form SS-4 has three questions specifically for LLCs. This allows EIN assignment employees to correctly assign the default filing requirements of Disregarded Entity or Partnership and populate the LLC>IND field on CC ESIGN. (3)
- A domestic LLC with two or more members is treated as a partnership by default. A domestic LLC can file Form 8832, Entity Classification Election, to avoid the default classification and elect to be classified as an association taxable as a corporation. (4)

- An LLC can also elect to be treated as an S corporation. For the S corporation status to be approved, Form 2553 must be received in the BMF Entity function according to the BMF Entity State Mapping chart. See IRM 21.7.13.7.2.2, Cases Forwarded to Submission Processing BMF Entity, (Form 8832 does not have to be filed if the LLC only wants to become an S corporation.) (5)
- Per Rev. Proc. 2002-69 and 2002 C.B. 831, spouses who are the sole owners of an LLC and reside in a community property state can choose whether they are treated as a partnership or disregarded entity. In either case, since these spouses are joint owners of the LLC, tax information related to the LLC can be discussed with either spouse. (6)

<span id="page-123-0"></span>**Note:** Community property states include: Arizona, California, Idaho, Louisiana, New Mexico, Nevada, Texas, Washington, and Wisconsin. Publication 555, Community Property, and IRM 21.8.1.16, Community Property, both contain additional information on community property laws.

### <span id="page-123-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.2.1 (01-13-2009)**

### **LLC Filing as a Corporation**

If the taxpayer has indicated Corporation on Line 9a, advise the taxpayer they must file Form 8832 to elect to be classified as an association taxable as a corporation, or Form 2553 under Rev. Proc. 2004–48 to elect S corporation status. If the taxpayer has a valid Power of Attorney, Taxpayer Information Authorization, or Third Party Designee, it is not necessary to provide this information. (1)

<span id="page-123-2"></span>**Note:** For EIN phones, advise taxpayer during the application process. Do not send Letter 147C to taxpayers applying by paper or fax since the CP 575 notice provides this information.

#### <span id="page-123-3"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.2.2 (01-13-2009)**

#### **LLC - Regulations Effective 1/1/2008 and 1/1/2009**

Final regulations changing the treatment of single-member LLCs (who have not filed an election to be taxed as a corporation) for employment and excise tax liabilities were issued on August 16, 2007. For certain excise tax liabilities (reported on Form 730, Form 2290, Form 11-C, and some Form 720 liabilities) incurred after January 1, 2008, the singlemember LLC is treated as a separate entity and is required to report (1)

excise taxes in the name and EIN of the LLC. For federal income tax purposes, the LLC is still disregarded. For employment tax liabilities incurred after January 1, 2009, the LLC will be treated as a separate entity and must report employment taxes in the name and EIN of the LLC. Again, the LLC will still be disregarded for federal income tax purposes.

- The changes effective January 1, 2008 required limited changes to procedures for EIN assignment. However, single-member LLCs without employees will not be discouraged from applying for an EIN, as they may require one for the reporting and payment of excise taxes. (2)
- Single-member LLCs who began paying employees **before** January 1, 2009 will need two EINs assigned to them. Assign one EIN to the owner (if they do not have one previously assigned) and assign another EIN to the LLC. (3)
- Single-member LLCs who will begin paying employees **after** January 1, 2009 will no longer require two EINs (one for the owner and one for the LLC). One EIN will be assigned to the LLC with the single-member's TIN in the SSN-ITIN-EIN> field. (4)

### <span id="page-124-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.3 (01-10-2008)**

### **Why Two EINs Are Assigned to a Single Member LLC for Certain Tax Periods**

- Two EINs were assigned to single-member LLCs with employees during tax periods ended prior to January 1, 2009 because: (1)
  - A single member LLC that is a disregarded entity (i.e., it has not filed an election to be taxed as a corporation) cannot be an employer. The owner is the employer of record. The employment tax regulations require that an employer must have an EIN.
  - Notice 99-6 allows a single member LLC that is a disregarded entity to calculate, report and pay employment taxes under the name and EIN of the LLC or the name and EIN of the owner. It was published at the request of practitioner groups who complained that without the option, disregarded entities would have to run parallel accounting systems for state and federal employment taxes. The state never disregarded the entity for tax purposes.

<span id="page-124-1"></span>**Note:** For tax periods beginning on or after January 1, 2009, Notice 99-6 is obsolete and employment taxes must be reported in the name and EIN of the LLC.

- If the taxpayer chooses to calculate, report, and pay their employment taxes under the LLC name for tax periods ended prior to January 1, 2009, assign two EINs (one for the owner and one for the disregarded entity). The taxpayer/preparer must make a concerted effort not to get the two confused. The two EINs will generate separate CP 575 notices. When processing fax, paper, or internet fallout applications, issue Letter 147C, advising that the owner EIN is just for cross-referencing purposes. (2)
- If the taxpayer chooses to calculate, report and pay their employment tax liabilities for tax periods ended prior to January 1, 2009 under the owner's name, and they are filing Form SS-4 to get an EIN for an LLC (for banking purposes or because their state requires an EIN for the LLC), they should not check "hired employees" in box 10. Instead, they should check banking purposes, or whatever is appropriate. (3)
- <span id="page-125-0"></span>See IRM 21.7.13.5.4.2.2, LLC - Regulations Effective 1/1/2008 and 1/1/2009, for changes effective January 1, 2009. (4)

### **21.7.13.5.4.3.1 (10-01-2020)**

#### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Single-Member LLC**

- By default, a domestic LLC with only one member is: (1)
  - Disregarded as an entity separate from its owner for federal income tax purposes except that it is subject to information reporting on Form 5472 for taxable years beginning after 12/31/2016, and
  - Must include all of its income and expenses on the owner's tax return
  - Disregarded as an entity separate from its owner for **all** other federal tax purposes except for employment taxes on wages paid on or after 1/1/2009 and certain excise taxes for periods beginning on or after 1/1/2008.
- (2) Research NAMEB and NAMEE to determine if the LLC had a previous EIN.
- (3) Use the table below to assign the EIN(s) and filing requirements:

<span id="page-126-1"></span><span id="page-126-0"></span>

| If                                                                                                                                                                                                   | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>The<br>LLC<br>is<br>disregarded<br>as<br>an<br>entity separate<br>from<br>its<br>owner<br>(for<br>federal<br>income<br>tax<br>purposes),<br>and<br>the<br>owner<br>is<br>an<br>individual      | Assign<br>the<br>EIN.<br>Establish<br>any known<br>excise<br>tax<br>filing<br>requirements<br>(2290,<br>730,<br>11-C)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN<br>if<br>the<br>BOD<br>is<br>1/1/2008<br>or<br>later.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| (and<br>does<br>not<br>have<br>employees)                                                                                                                                                            | Note:<br>The<br>owner<br>of<br>the<br>disregarded<br>LLC<br>is<br>responsible<br>for<br>all<br>federal<br>income<br>tax<br>filings<br>(Form<br>1040)<br>using<br>their<br>SSN<br>or<br>ITIN.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.4.2.2,<br>LLC<br>-<br>Regulations<br>Effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009,<br>for<br>changes<br>effective<br>1/1/2008.                                                                                                                                                                        |
| 2)<br>The<br>owner<br>is<br>an<br>entity<br>that<br>is<br>not<br>an<br>individual<br>(e.g.,<br>corporation,<br>trust,<br>estate,<br>partnership,<br>etc.)<br>and<br>does<br>not<br>have<br>employees | Assign<br>the<br>EIN<br>Note:<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.4.2.2,<br>LLC<br>-<br>Regulations<br>Effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009,<br>for<br>changes<br>effective<br>1/1/2008.<br>Input<br>the<br>owner's<br>name<br>in<br>the<br>in<br>care-of<br>field<br>followed<br>by MBR<br>or<br>Single/Sole<br>MBR.<br>Establish<br>any known<br>excise<br>tax<br>filing<br>requirements<br>(Form<br>2290,<br>Form<br>730,<br>Form<br>11-C)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN<br>if<br>the<br>BOD<br>is<br>1/1/2008<br>or<br>later. |

<span id="page-127-0"></span>

| If                                                                                                                                                                                            | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 3)<br>The<br>LLC<br>is<br>disregarded<br>(individual<br>owner<br>or<br>other<br>entity),<br>and<br>has<br>employees<br>during<br>tax<br>periods<br>ended<br>prior<br>to<br>January 1,<br>2009 | The<br>owner<br>must<br>have<br>a<br>separate<br>EIN<br>for<br>the<br>LLC,<br>unless<br>they choose<br>to<br>file<br>under<br>the<br>owner's<br>name<br>and<br>TIN.<br>In<br>the<br>case<br>of<br>an<br>individual,<br>they<br>would<br>use<br>the<br>sole<br>proprietor<br>EIN.<br>In<br>the<br>case<br>of<br>an<br>entity,<br>they would<br>use<br>the<br>EIN<br>of<br>the<br>single<br>owner<br>(ex.<br>Corp).<br>See<br>IRM<br>3.13.2.26,<br>Domestic<br>Limited<br>Liability Company (LLC),<br>for<br>more<br>information.<br>If<br>the<br>owner<br>chooses<br>to<br>obtain<br>a<br>separate<br>EIN<br>for<br>the<br>LLC,<br>then<br>the<br>individual<br>owner<br>must<br>have<br>an<br>EIN<br>that<br>will<br>in<br>turn<br>be<br>used<br>as<br>a<br>cross-reference<br>for<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN.<br>Follow |
|                                                                                                                                                                                               | the<br>four<br>steps<br>below:<br>a.<br>Assign<br>an<br>EIN<br>to<br>the<br>owner,<br>if<br>they do<br>not<br>already have<br>one.<br>b.<br>Assign<br>the<br>second<br>EIN<br>to<br>the<br>LLC.<br>c.<br>Establish<br>filing<br>requirements<br>for<br>employment<br>taxes<br>for<br>the<br>owner's<br>EIN<br>or<br>LLC's<br>EIN,<br>as<br>indicated<br>by the<br>taxpayer<br>for<br>tax<br>periods<br>ended<br>prior<br>to<br>1/1/2009.<br>d.<br>Inform<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>by sending<br>Letter<br>147C,<br>indicating<br>that<br>they have<br>been<br>assigned<br>two<br>EINs;<br>one<br>for<br>the<br>owner,<br>and<br>one<br>for<br>the<br>LLC.                                                                                                                                                             |
|                                                                                                                                                                                               | Note:<br>Third<br>Party Designees<br>applying<br>for<br>an<br>EIN<br>for<br>a<br>single-member<br>LLC<br>with<br>employees<br>are<br>authorized<br>to<br>receive<br>both<br>the<br>owner's<br>EIN<br>and<br>the<br>LLC's<br>EIN.<br>Exception:<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.4.2.2,<br>LLC<br>-<br>Regulations<br>Effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009,<br>for<br>changes<br>effective<br>1/1/2009.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |

<span id="page-128-0"></span>

| If                                                                                                                                                                                                       | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 4)<br>The<br>LLC<br>has<br>employees<br>for<br>tax<br>periods<br>beginning<br>on<br>or<br>after<br>January 1,<br>2009<br>and<br>the<br>owner<br>is<br>an<br>individual                                   | Assign<br>the<br>EIN.<br>Establish<br>any known<br>excise<br>tax<br>filing<br>requirements<br>(Form<br>2290,<br>Form<br>730,<br>Form<br>11-C)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN.<br>Establish<br>filing<br>requirements<br>for<br>employment<br>taxes<br>(94X)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                              |
|                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Note:<br>The<br>owner<br>of<br>the<br>disregarded<br>LLC<br>is<br>responsible<br>for<br>all<br>federal<br>income<br>tax<br>filings<br>(Form<br>1040<br>including<br>all<br>schedules,<br>Form<br>1099,<br>Form<br>W-9,<br>etc.)<br>using<br>their<br>SSN<br>or<br>ITIN.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.4.2.2,<br>LLC<br>-<br>Regulations<br>Effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009,<br>for<br>changes<br>effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009. |
| 5)<br>The<br>LLC<br>has<br>employees<br>for<br>tax<br>periods<br>beginning<br>on<br>or<br>after<br>January 1,<br>2009<br>and<br>the<br>owner<br>is<br>an<br>entity that<br>is<br>not<br>an<br>individual | Assign<br>the<br>EIN.<br>Establish<br>any known<br>excise<br>tax<br>filing<br>requirements<br>(Form<br>2290,<br>Form<br>730,<br>Form<br>11-C)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN.<br>Establish<br>filing<br>requirements<br>for<br>employment<br>taxes<br>(94X)<br>on<br>the<br>LLC<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                              |
|                                                                                                                                                                                                          | Note:<br>The<br>owner<br>of<br>the<br>disregarded<br>LLC<br>is<br>responsible<br>for<br>all<br>other<br>federal<br>tax<br>filings<br>(Form<br>1065,<br>Form<br>1120,<br>Form<br>1099,<br>Form<br>W<br>9,<br>etc.)<br>using<br>the<br>EIN<br>for<br>the<br>entity.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.4.2.2,<br>LLC<br>-<br>Regulations<br>Effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009,<br>for<br>changes<br>effective<br>1/1/2008<br>and<br>1/1/2009.       |

#### <span id="page-128-2"></span><span id="page-128-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.4 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: LLC**

Tax information must be disclosed in conformance with the Federal tax treatment of the LLC. See IRM 11.3.2.4, Persons Who May Have Access to Returns and Return Information Pursuant to IRC 6103(e). For AM EIN (1)

<span id="page-129-0"></span>assignment purposes, default classification rules for LLCs apply. See the table below for additional information.

**Note:** A third party, authorized by the taxpayer, would also be authorized to receive the EIN.

<span id="page-129-1"></span>

|                             | The<br>Default<br>Tax     |                                            |
|-----------------------------|---------------------------|--------------------------------------------|
| If<br>the<br>LLC<br>is<br>a | Classification<br>is      | Then                                       |
| 1)<br>Multi-Member          | Partnership               | Any of<br>the<br>LLC<br>members            |
|                             |                           | (who<br>are<br>treated<br>as<br>partners   |
|                             |                           | for<br>Federal<br>tax<br>purposes)         |
|                             |                           | can<br>receive<br>the<br>EIN.              |
| 2)<br>Single                | Disregarded<br>Entity for | The<br>individual<br>owner<br>is           |
| Member<br>(Owned            | Federal<br>Income<br>Tax  | authorized<br>to<br>receive<br>the         |
| by an<br>individual)        | Purposes                  | EIN.                                       |
| 3)<br>Single                | Disregarded<br>Entity for | The<br>EIN<br>can<br>be<br>disclosed<br>to |
| Member<br>(Owned            | Federal<br>Income<br>Tax  | a<br>person<br>who<br>is<br>authorized     |
| by a<br>business            | Purposes                  | to<br>receive<br>tax<br>information        |
| entity)                     |                           | for<br>that<br>business<br>entity.         |
|                             |                           | Example:<br>If<br>the<br>LLC<br>is         |
|                             |                           | owned<br>by The<br>Flamingo                |
|                             |                           | Corp,<br>follow<br>the<br>rules<br>for     |
|                             |                           | disclosure<br>to<br>corporations.          |

#### <span id="page-129-2"></span>**21.7.13.5.4.5 (04-23-2019)**

### **CC ESIGN Input: LLC**

The table below describes the fields and the entries for LLCs. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3, CC ESIGN Input Screen, for general input instructions. (1)

<span id="page-129-3"></span>

| Field                  | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                               |
|------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Master<br>File<br>Ind. | MFI<br>is<br>O<br>if<br>no<br>filing<br>requirements;<br>B<br>if<br>filing       |
|                        | requirements.                                                                    |
| Loc-Cd                 | Input<br>the<br>valid<br>two-digit<br>EIN<br>prefix<br>for<br>the<br>campus.     |
|                        | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.2.4,<br>How<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Assigned.                |
|                        | Note:<br>The<br>last<br>two<br>positions<br>of<br>the<br>field<br>display<br>the |
|                        | Area<br>Office<br>Code<br>(00).                                                  |
| Name-Ctrl              | The<br>Name<br>Control<br>is<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>characters<br>of<br>the  |
|                        | LLC<br>name.<br>Follow<br>corporate<br>name<br>control<br>rules<br>if            |
|                        | "the"<br>is<br>the<br>first<br>word<br>in<br>the<br>LLC<br>name.<br>See<br>IRM   |
|                        | 21.7.13.5.2.6,<br>CC<br>ESIGN<br>Input:<br>Corporations.                         |

<span id="page-130-1"></span><span id="page-130-0"></span>

| Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |  |
|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| The<br>Primary Name<br>is<br>the<br>name<br>of<br>the<br>LLC<br>as<br>it<br>appears<br>on<br>the<br>articles<br>of<br>organization<br>by<br>the<br>state.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |  |
| Delete<br>the<br>word<br>"the"<br>,<br>unless<br>it<br>is<br>followed<br>by only one<br>word.<br>Otherwise,<br>do<br>not<br>modify the<br>LLC's<br>name.<br>Do<br>not<br>abbreviate,<br>change<br>symbols,<br>or<br>change<br>"and"<br>to<br>"&"<br>The<br>ampersand<br>(&)<br>and<br>the<br>hyphen<br>(-)<br>are<br>considered<br>valid<br>characters<br>in<br>the<br>Primary<br>Name<br>line.<br>Suffixes<br>such<br>as<br>LLC,<br>LC,<br>and<br>PLLC<br>(or<br>LLP<br>for<br>a<br>limited<br>liability partnership)<br>indicate<br>a<br>limited<br>liability company and<br>are<br>input<br>with<br>the<br>LLC's<br>name.<br>Note:<br>Do<br>not<br>add<br>an<br>LLC<br>suffix<br>to<br>the<br>name<br>line<br>if<br>one<br>is<br>not<br>present. |  |
| The<br>Sort<br>Name<br>is<br>the<br>doing<br>business<br>as<br>(DBA)<br>name,<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>different<br>from<br>the<br>true<br>or<br>legal<br>name.<br>Note:<br>If<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>supplies<br>a<br>member's<br>name<br>and<br>there<br>is<br>not<br>a<br>DBA<br>name,<br>enter<br>the<br>individual's<br>name<br>followed<br>by the<br>abbreviations,<br>mbr<br>or<br>single<br>(or<br>sole)<br>mbr.<br>Never<br>input<br>LLC<br>name<br>in<br>the<br>sort<br>line.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.4.2,<br>Sort<br>Name<br>Input<br>Field<br>Requirements,<br>for<br>input<br>information.                                                                                                                                           |  |
| The<br>In-Care<br>of<br>Name<br>is<br>the<br>name<br>of<br>the<br>member<br>or<br>single<br>member<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>provided<br>and<br>was<br>not<br>used<br>as<br>the<br>Sort<br>Name.<br>Exception:<br>If<br>the<br>Primary Name<br>is<br>identical<br>to<br>the<br>In-Care-of-Name,<br>this<br>field<br>is<br>not<br>required.<br>If<br>another<br>entity is<br>listed<br>as<br>a<br>member<br>(e.g.,<br>a<br>trust,<br>a<br>corporation,<br>another<br>LLC<br>or<br>a<br>partnership),<br>enter<br>it<br>as<br>the<br>In-Care-of-Name<br>followed<br>by mbr<br>or<br>single<br>(or<br>sole)<br>mbr.<br>If<br>the<br>Primary Name<br>is<br>identical<br>to<br>the<br>In<br>Care-of-Name,<br>this<br>field<br>is<br>not<br>required.          |  |
| See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.2,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP<br>Field.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |  |

#### <span id="page-133-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.5 (03-02-2018)**

### **EIN Assignment: Non-Profit/Exempt**

<span id="page-133-1"></span>This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for non-profit and exempt organizations. (1)

#### **21.7.13.5.5.1 (04-04-2007)**

### **Definition: Non-Profit/Exempt**

- Non-profit status is a state law concept. Non-profit status may make an organization eligible for certain benefits, such as state sales, property, and income tax exemptions. Although most federal tax-exempt organizations are non-profit organizations, organizing as a non-profit organization at the state level does not automatically grant the organization exemption from federal income tax. To qualify as exempt from federal income taxes, an organization must meet requirements set forth in the Internal Revenue Code. (1)
- Non-profit organizations include both tax exempt organizations and government entities. The following list is an example of some of these entities. This list is not all-inclusive: (2)

- Business leagues
- Charitable organizations
- Educational organizations
- Employee associations
- Farmers' cooperative
- Federal government/military
- Indian tribal governments/enterprises
- Private foundations
- Religious organizations
- Social clubs
- State-chartered credit unions
- State/local government
- Teachers' retirement fund associations
- Veterans organizations
- <span id="page-134-0"></span>For more information on non-profit and exempt organizations, see IRM 3.13.12, Exempt Organization Account Numbers. (3)

#### **21.7.13.5.5.2 (10-01-2022)**

### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Non-Profit/Exempt**

- The EIN of a tax exempt organization which is not publicly available under IRC 6104 may be disclosed to any person legally authorized to act for the organization. (1)
- Organizations can have varying names for titles of officers. The key is to establish that the person with whom you are in contact is legally authorized to act on behalf of the organization. (2)
- Ask the caller for their name, SSN/ITIN, address and DOB. Also ask the following question: "Are you a current officer or director legally authorized to act on behalf of the organization/plan?" (3)
- EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (4)

#### <span id="page-134-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.5.3 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: Non-Profit/Exempt**

Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 (1)

below when performing research.

When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number: (2)

<span id="page-135-0"></span>

| Step | Action                                                                                       |
|------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1    | Research<br>the<br>primary name<br>to<br>ensure<br>an<br>EIN<br>does<br>not<br>already       |
|      | exist<br>for<br>that<br>organization<br>using:                                               |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB<br>and                                                                           |
|      | CC<br>NAMEE                                                                                  |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                        |
|      | Note:<br>If<br>provided,<br>verify the<br>cross<br>reference<br>SSN<br>or<br>ITIN<br>from    |
|      | Line<br>7b<br>of<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>using<br>CC<br>INOLE.<br>(Exempt<br>organizations<br>are |
|      | not<br>required<br>to<br>provide<br>cross<br>reference<br>SSN/EIN<br>information.            |
|      | However,<br>many taxpayers<br>supply this<br>information.)                                   |
| 2    | Were<br>you<br>able<br>to<br>locate<br>the<br>non-profit/exempt<br>organization's            |
|      | EIN?                                                                                         |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>go<br>to<br>Step<br>3.                                                         |
|      | If<br>no,<br>research<br>the<br>sort<br>or<br>trade<br>name<br>if<br>available.              |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                             |
|      |                                                                                              |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM         |
|      | 21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.                               |
|      | If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>with<br>assigning<br>an<br>EIN.                                      |

#### <span id="page-135-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.5.4 (10-01-2007)**

### **Determining Tax Classification and Employment Code: Non-Profit/Exempt**

- Most incorporated exempt organizations file one of the Form 990 series returns and should always be established on the "O" file. Do not assign 990 filing requirements. (1)
- Non-profit organizations include corporations, trusts, limited liability companies, and unincorporated associations that qualify for tax-exempt status under IRC 501(a) as described in Publication 557, Tax-Exempt Status for Your Organization. Sole proprietors and partnerships cannot be considered for tax exempt status. (2)

<span id="page-135-2"></span>**Note:** If any of the entity types listed in paragraph (2) select "Other nonprofit organization" as their type of entity, establish the entity on the "O" file.

<span id="page-136-0"></span>**Exception:** If a political organization indicates on Form SS-4 that it is requesting an EIN under Section 527 or filing Form 8871, Political Organization Notice of Section 527 Status, enter the Master File Indicator of **B**, input a "1" in the POL-ORG field, and establish a Form 1120-09 filing requirement on CC ESIGN.

Use the table below to determine the correct employment code. See IRM 21.7.13.7.4, BMF Employment Codes for Non-Profit/Exempt Entities, for detailed descriptions of Employment Codes and IRM 21.7.13.7.3.11, Employment Code Input, for Employment Code input instructions. (3)

| Organization                                                                     | Employment<br>Code |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------|
| United<br>States<br>Government<br>agencies                                       | F                  |
| State<br>and<br>local<br>government<br>agencies                                  | G                  |
| Non-profit<br>organizations<br>as<br>described<br>in<br>Sections                 | W                  |
| 501(c)(3),<br>501(e),<br>501(f),<br>and<br>501(k)<br>of<br>the<br>IRC            |                    |
| Note:<br>Input<br>a<br>941,<br>943,<br>or<br>944<br>filing<br>requirement,<br>if |                    |
| appropriate.                                                                     |                    |

#### <span id="page-140-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.5.6 (10-01-2022)**

### **Group Exemption Number: Non-profit/Exempt**

- When a non-profit organization indicates a Group Exemption Number (GEN) on Line 9a of Form SS-4, assign the EIN on the "O" file but do not establish the EO submodule or add the GEN, unless the Form SS-4 is either submitted by the parent organization or a group exemption letter is attached to the application listing the new entity as a subordinate. (1)
- The parent or central organization must request the subordinate be added to its group exemption. The parent organization can do this at any time during the year by providing the required information to the EO Entity group at the Ogden campus. See IRM 21.3.8.12.14.5, Adding Subordinates to a Group Exemption and Modifying Subordinate Information, for additional information. (2)

- Central organizations, with the exception of churches, are required annually to provide a current listing of information on themselves and their subordinate units. See IRM 25.7.1.9.1, Supplemental Group Ruling Information (SGRI), for additional information. (3)
- <span id="page-141-0"></span>If one of the conditions in paragraph (1) is met, follow the instructions in IRM 3.13.12.12.10.4.5, Adding a Subordinate. (4)

#### **21.7.13.5.6 (03-02-2018)**

#### <span id="page-141-1"></span>**EIN Assignment: Estate**

(1) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for Estates.

#### **21.7.13.5.6.1 (10-01-2013)**

#### **Definition: Estates**

<span id="page-141-2"></span>An estate is a legal entity created as a result of a person's death. The estate consists of the real property and other assets of the deceased person. (1)

**Caution:** Do not assign an EIN if the named (deceased person) is not deceased and is applying for a decedent estate. A decedent estate does not exist until the person for whom the estate EIN is being requested is deceased.

<span id="page-141-3"></span>The estate pays any debts owed by the decedent and distributes the balance of the estate's assets to the beneficiaries of the estate. (2)

#### **21.7.13.5.6.2 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Estates**

<span id="page-141-4"></span>Established EINs can be disclosed to a fiduciary of the estate (administrator, executor, or personal representative) or to an authorized third party. (1)

**Note:** Authentication of the individual must be verified using CC INOLE.

Do not disclose an EIN to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)

#### **21.7.13.5.6.3 (10-01-2005)**

**Determining the Need for an EIN: Estates**

Use the table below to determine the need for an EIN for estates. (1)

| If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>requested                                         | Then<br>a<br>new<br>EIN<br>is |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------|
| 1)<br>As<br>a<br>result<br>of<br>a<br>person's<br>death                    | Needed.                       |
| 2)<br>Because<br>the<br>beneficiaries<br>or<br>the<br>executor<br>of<br>an | Not<br>needed.                |
| estate<br>changes                                                          |                               |

#### <span id="page-142-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.6.4 (11-18-2024)**

### **Required Taxpayer Information: Estates**

- Form SS-4 should include the following: (1)
  - The name of the decedent followed by the word "estate" on Line 1.
  - The estate box checked on Line 9a and decedent's SSN or ITIN.

#### **21.7.13.5.6.5 (10-01-2008)**

#### **6/7 Million Series EINs: Estates**

<span id="page-142-1"></span>Based on the Master File indicator (MFI) and filing requirement input, the EIN Research and Assignment System (ERAS) generates a 6/7 million series EIN for estates (the filing requirement is a 1041 with no other filing requirements). (1)

**Note:** Immediately following the dash, the third digit of the estate EIN is a six or seven.

- The 6/7 million series is used for MFI of B with a 1041 FR and for accounts under the Tax Equity and Fiscal Responsibility Act (TEFRA). (2)
- <span id="page-142-2"></span>An appropriate EIN is selected from the EIN Assignment Control File (EACF). (3)

**Exception:** If employment tax filing requirements are present, a regular series EIN will be assigned to the estate.

#### <span id="page-142-3"></span>**21.7.13.5.6.6 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: Estates**

Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool researches all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)

When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

| Step | Action                                                                |
|------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1    | Verify decedent's<br>SSN<br>or<br>ITIN<br>using:                      |
|      | CC<br>INOLE                                                           |
|      | CC<br>NAMEI                                                           |
|      | CC<br>NAMES                                                           |
| 2    | Research<br>the<br>estate's<br>primary name<br>and<br>executor<br>or  |
|      | representative's<br>name,<br>if<br>available,<br>using:               |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB                                                           |
|      | CC<br>NAMEE                                                           |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information. |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                      |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.3,<br>Research<br>Using<br>CC<br>ENMOD      |
|      | (Taxpayer<br>Information<br>File).                                    |
|      | If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.     |

#### <span id="page-147-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.6.8 (10-01-2007)**

### **Additional Filing Information: Estates**

- The taxpayer can report and pay Federal Insurance Contribution Act (FICA), Federal Unemployment Tax Act (FUTA), and any income tax withholding for household employees on Form 1041, by attaching Form 1040, Schedule H. (1)
- If the taxpayer owns their own company, and previously reported household employees on Form 940 and/or Form 941, other employees plus household employees can be reported on Form 940 and/or Form 941. (2)

### **21.7.13.5.7 (03-02-2018)**

### <span id="page-147-1"></span>**EIN Assignment: Employee Plans**

(1) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for plans.

#### **21.7.13.5.7.1 (10-01-2013)**

#### **Definitions: Employee Plans**

The table below describes some of the different types of plans. (1)

| Plan<br>Type  | Definition                                                                             |
|---------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| SIMPLE<br>IRA | A<br>SIMPLE<br>IRA<br>plan<br>is<br>a<br>Savings<br>Incentive<br>Match<br>PLan<br>for  |
|               | Employees.<br>Under<br>a<br>SIMPLE<br>IRA<br>plan,<br>employees<br>and                 |
|               | employers<br>make<br>contributions<br>to<br>traditional<br>Individual                  |
|               | Retirement<br>Arrangements<br>(IRAs)<br>set<br>up<br>for<br>employees                  |
|               | (including<br>self-employed<br>individuals),<br>subject<br>to<br>certain               |
|               | limits.<br>A<br>SIMPLE<br>IRA<br>Plan<br>is<br>funded<br>both<br>by<br>employer<br>and |
|               | employee<br>contributions.                                                             |

| Definition                                                                             |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| A<br>SIMPLE<br>401(k)<br>plan<br>is<br>a<br>Savings<br>Incentive<br>Match<br>PLan      |
| for<br>Employees.<br>A<br>SIMPLE<br>plan<br>can<br>be<br>adopted<br>as<br>part<br>of   |
| a<br>401(k)<br>plan<br>if<br>the<br>employer<br>has<br>100<br>or<br>fewer              |
| employees.<br>A<br>SIMPLE<br>401(k)<br>plan<br>is<br>funded<br>both<br>by              |
| employer<br>and<br>employee<br>contributions                                           |
| A<br>SEP<br>is<br>a<br>Simplified<br>Employee<br>Pension<br>plan.<br>Under<br>a        |
| SEP,<br>employers<br>make<br>contributions<br>to<br>traditional                        |
| Individual<br>Retirement<br>Arrangements<br>(IRAs)<br>set<br>up<br>for                 |
| employees<br>(including<br>self-employed<br>individuals),<br>subject                   |
| to<br>certain<br>limits.<br>A<br>SEP<br>is<br>funded<br>solely by<br>employer          |
| contributions.                                                                         |
| A<br>Keogh<br>plan<br>refers<br>to<br>a<br>qualified<br>pension<br>plan                |
| maintained<br>by self<br>employed<br>individuals<br>that<br>may<br>be                  |
| designed<br>as<br>either<br>a<br>defined<br>benefit<br>or<br>a<br>defined              |
| contribution<br>plan.<br>A<br>sole<br>proprietor<br>or<br>a<br>partnership<br>can      |
| set<br>up<br>one<br>of<br>these<br>plans.<br>A<br>common<br>law<br>employee<br>or<br>a |
| partner<br>cannot<br>set<br>up<br>one<br>of<br>these<br>plans.                         |
| A<br>qualified<br>defined<br>contribution<br>plan<br>under<br>which<br>the             |
| plan<br>may provide<br>or<br>the<br>employer<br>may<br>determine                       |
| annually how<br>much<br>will<br>be<br>contributed<br>to<br>the<br>plan<br>(out         |
| of<br>profits<br>or<br>otherwise).                                                     |
| A<br>type<br>of<br>qualified<br>retirement<br>plan<br>through<br>which<br>the          |
| employer<br>contributes<br>to<br>a<br>fund<br>to<br>provide<br>employees               |
| with<br>definitely determinable<br>benefits<br>over<br>a<br>period<br>of               |
| years<br>(usually for<br>life)<br>after<br>retirement.                                 |
| A<br>defined<br>contribution<br>plan<br>under<br>which<br>an<br>employer               |
| makes<br>fixed<br>contributions<br>to<br>separate<br>accounts<br>for<br>the            |
| plan<br>participants.                                                                  |
|                                                                                        |
| A<br>qualified<br>defined<br>contribution<br>plan<br>established<br>by                 |
| employers<br>to<br>which<br>eligible<br>employees<br>may<br>make<br>salary             |
| deferral<br>(salary reduction)<br>contributions<br>on<br>a<br>post-tax                 |
| and/or<br>pretax<br>basis.<br>Employers<br>may make<br>matching<br>or                  |
| nonelective<br>contributions<br>to<br>the<br>plan<br>on<br>behalf<br>of                |
| eligible<br>employees<br>and<br>may also<br>add<br>a<br>profit-sharing                 |
| feature<br>to<br>the<br>plan.                                                          |
|                                                                                        |

<span id="page-148-0"></span>**Note:** A traditional Individual Retirement Arrangement or IRA is not an Employee Plan. A traditional IRA is a personal savings plan which allows individuals to set aside money for retirement, while offering tax advantages. Some or all contributions to the IRA may be deductible. Amounts in the IRA, including earnings, generally are not taxed until distributed. IRA's cannot be owned jointly. An individual does not need an EIN to establish a traditional IRA.

#### <span id="page-149-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.2 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Additional Information for Employee Plans**

<span id="page-149-1"></span>For more information on employee plans account numbers, see IRM 3.13.36, EPMF Account Numbers. (1)

#### **21.7.13.5.7.3 (10-01-2013)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Employee Plans**

- IRA or Keogh established EINs can only be disclosed to: (1)
  - The individual person, or
  - An authorized third party representative
- Pension, profit sharing, 401(k), or welfare benefit plan established EINs can only be disclosed to: (2)
  - The Trustee of the plan
  - Plan administrator
  - Grantor, or
  - Authorized third party representative
- EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (3)

#### <span id="page-149-2"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.4 (10-01-2007)**

#### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Employee Plans**

- An EIN is needed if the: (1)
  - Plan is a permanent arrangement under which an employer provides benefits for employees, or
  - Employer/sponsor and/or the plan file the applicable returns

<span id="page-150-0"></span>An IRA trust does not require an EIN, unless it has to file Form 990-T or Form 1041. (2)

**Note:** A sole proprietor, who has not previously applied for an EIN, may attempt to open a retirement account that is available to self-employed persons, such as a Keogh plan. The bank or financial institution will advise the taxpayer they must have an EIN to do this. The taxpayer may say they are applying for a Keogh, or IRA EIN, when in fact, all they need is a sole proprietor EIN. Be alert to this situation and explain to the taxpayer that you will be assigning them an EIN as a sole proprietor and they should use this EIN for all their business needs, including opening retirement accounts that are available to self-employed persons.

#### <span id="page-150-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.5 (10-01-2005)**

### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: Employee Plans**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |  |
|------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 1    | Determine<br>whether<br>the<br>plan<br>already has<br>an<br>EIN<br>by<br>using:                                                                                                                                             |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB,<br>and<br>CC<br>NAMEE.                                                                                                                                                                                         |  |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                       |  |
| 2    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                            |  |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN. |  |

#### <span id="page-150-2"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.5.1 (10-01-2013)**

#### **Additional Research for Pension Plans**

- Research the plan name if the taxpayer, on Form SS-4: (1)
  - Indicates a pension plan on Line 1
  - Checks the trust box on Line 9a, or
  - Checks the plan administrator box on Line 9a, and

Checks the Created a pension plan box on Line 10

#### <span id="page-151-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.5.2 (10-01-2019)**

### **Additional Research for Financial Institutions: Employee Plans**

- If a financial institution requests an EIN for the purpose of reporting withholding from Individual Retirement Accounts (IRAs), IRA Rollover Trusts, or Keogh plans (HR10), research to determine if an EIN has been assigned previously for the purpose of reporting for pension trusts under their authority. (1)
- This number will be a six million series number and the account may or may not have the second name line annotated "Account Under TEFRA" . If a number has been assigned previously, correspond with the applicant informing them that only one EIN will be assigned for the purpose of reporting withholding under TEFRA for multiple plans. They may report withholding for the plans which they administer, or act as payer under this number, or IRA accounts can be reported under the EIN of the financial institution and aggregated on their Form 945. Inform them of the correct number to use. (2)

<span id="page-151-1"></span>**Note:** TEFRA is no longer effective for partnership taxable years beginning after December 31, 2017.

#### <span id="page-151-2"></span>**21.7.13.5.7.6 (04-23-2019)**

|-------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>For<br>a<br>plan<br>administrator<br>or<br>plan | O<br>with<br>no<br>filing<br>requirements. |
| administrative<br>committee                           |                                            |
| 2)<br>For<br>an<br>employee<br>benefit                | O<br>with<br>no<br>filing<br>requirements. |
| funds/trust<br>without<br>employees                   |                                            |

| If<br>the<br>entity<br>type<br>is                      | Then<br>the<br>MFI<br>is                           |
|--------------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------|

| funds/trust<br>that                                    | (if<br>appropriate)<br>filing                      |

| funds/trust,<br>and<br>the<br>taxpayer                 | requirement<br>of<br>1.                            |
| indicates<br>that<br>the<br>application<br>is<br>being | Note:<br>If<br>a<br>previously assigned            |
| submitted<br>to<br>comply with<br>the                  | EIN<br>has<br>fallen<br>off<br>the<br>system       |
| requirements<br>of<br>the<br>Tax<br>Equity and         | due<br>to<br>inactivity,<br>reestablish            |
