#### <span id="page-156-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.8 (03-02-2018)**

#### <span id="page-156-1"></span>**EIN Assignment: Trusts**

(1) This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for trusts.

#### **21.7.13.5.8.1 (10-01-2017)**

#### **Definition: Trusts**

- A trust is a legal entity that: (1)
  - Is created under State law
  - Is taxed under federal law in which one party holds assets for the benefit of another, and
  - Can be created to do one act or a series of acts.
- The table below describes associated terms and types of trusts. (2)

| Term          | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|---------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Fiduciary     | Trustee<br>of<br>a<br>trust,<br>or<br>Executor,<br>executrix,<br>administrator,<br>administratrix,<br>personal<br>representative,<br>or<br>person<br>in<br>possession<br>of<br>a<br>property of<br>a<br>decedent |
| Beneficiary   | A<br>person<br>designated<br>as<br>the<br>recipient<br>of<br>funds<br>or<br>other<br>property under<br>a<br>trust<br>or<br>an<br>estate                                                                          |
| Corpus        | The<br>principal<br>sum<br>of<br>the<br>capital<br>of<br>a<br>trust<br>or<br>an<br>estate,<br>as<br>distinguished<br>from<br>interest<br>or<br>income                                                            |
| Maker/grantor | The<br>person(s)<br>or<br>organization<br>that<br>Originated<br>the<br>trust,<br>or<br>Has<br>control<br>over<br>the<br>trust                                                                                    |

<span id="page-157-1"></span><span id="page-157-0"></span>

| Term                    | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|-------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Simple<br>Trust         | A<br>trust                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|                         | For<br>which<br>the<br>trust<br>instrument<br>requires<br>that<br>all<br>income<br>be<br>distributed<br>currently,<br>with<br>no<br>authority to<br>make<br>charitable<br>contributions<br>or<br>distribute<br>amounts<br>allocated<br>to<br>the<br>corpus<br>of<br>the<br>trust,<br>and<br>That<br>is<br>a<br>simple<br>trust<br>only for<br>a<br>year<br>in<br>which<br>it<br>distributes<br>income<br>and<br>makes<br>no<br>other<br>distributions<br>to<br>beneficiaries<br>Note:<br>When<br>a<br>trust<br>does<br>not<br>meet<br>these<br>requirements<br>for<br>a<br>year,<br>it<br>is<br>a<br>complex<br>trust.                           |
| Complex<br>Trust        | A<br>trust<br>which,<br>for<br>the<br>taxable<br>year,                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|                         | does<br>not<br>qualify as<br>a<br>simple<br>trust                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Grantor<br>Trust        | A<br>trust<br>is<br>set<br>up<br>by a<br>living<br>person<br>or<br>organization,<br>or<br>created<br>by a<br>will<br>where<br>grantor<br>retains<br>certain<br>powers<br>or<br>ownership<br>benefits<br>or<br>Is<br>set<br>up<br>so<br>that<br>the<br>income<br>from<br>the<br>trust<br>is<br>taxable<br>income<br>of<br>the<br>grantor<br>Non-taxable<br>grantor<br>trusts<br>do<br>not<br>report<br>income,<br>deductions,<br>and<br>credits<br>on<br>Form<br>1041,<br>U.S.<br>Income<br>Tax<br>Return<br>for<br>Trusts<br>and<br>Estates.<br>Note:<br>The<br>grantor<br>may file<br>Form<br>1041<br>for<br>informational<br>purposes<br>only. |
| Inter<br>vivos<br>Trust | A<br>trust<br>established<br>by a<br>grantor<br>during<br>their<br>lifetime.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

<span id="page-158-0"></span>

| Term                 | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |  |
|----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| Revocable<br>Trust   | The<br>grantor:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |  |
|                      | Has<br>control<br>of<br>the<br>trust<br>(e.g.,<br>has<br>power<br>to<br>repeal<br>or<br>annul),<br>and<br>Pays<br>the<br>taxes<br>of<br>the<br>trust<br>on<br>their<br>Form<br>1040,<br>U.S.<br>Individual<br>Income<br>Tax<br>Return<br>Note:<br>The<br>grantor<br>files<br>Form<br>1041<br>for<br>informational<br>purposes<br>only.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |  |
| Irrevocable<br>Trust | An<br>irrevocable<br>trust<br>is<br>a<br>trust<br>in<br>which<br>the<br>grantor<br>has<br>no<br>control<br>of<br>the<br>trust<br>(trust<br>cannot<br>be<br>repealed<br>or<br>annulled)<br>and<br>the<br>trust<br>is<br>responsible<br>for<br>reporting<br>income<br>on<br>Form<br>1041,<br>U.S.<br>Income<br>Tax<br>Return<br>for<br>Estates<br>and<br>Trusts.                                                                                                                                                                                                             |  |
| Testamentary Trust   | A<br>testamentary trust<br>is<br>created<br>by a<br>will,<br>which<br>begins<br>its<br>existence<br>upon<br>the<br>death<br>of<br>the<br>person<br>making<br>the<br>will,<br>when<br>property is<br>transferred<br>from<br>the<br>decedent's<br>estate.<br>Testamentary<br>trusts<br>are<br>generally simple<br>or<br>complex<br>trusts.<br>A<br>testamentary trust<br>is<br>irrevocable<br>by definition,<br>as<br>it<br>comes<br>into<br>being<br>at<br>the<br>death<br>of<br>the<br>grantor.<br>It<br>is<br>also<br>known<br>as<br>a<br>"trust<br>under<br>the<br>will" |  |
| Residual<br>Trust    | A<br>trust<br>set<br>up<br>to<br>receive<br>the<br>part<br>of<br>an<br>estate<br>that<br>remains<br>after<br>the<br>payment<br>of<br>all<br>debts,<br>charges,<br>devices,<br>and<br>bequests<br>to<br>entities<br>other<br>than<br>the<br>beneficiary                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |  |

<span id="page-159-0"></span>

| Term                                                                             | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Conservatorship                                                                  | A<br>conservatorship<br>is:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|                                                                                  | A<br>trust<br>set<br>up<br>for<br>an<br>incompetent<br>person<br>and<br>created<br>by a<br>court<br>order<br>subjecting<br>property or<br>a<br>person<br>to<br>the<br>legal<br>control<br>of<br>another<br>person<br>or<br>entity.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Guardianship/Custodianship                                                       | A<br>trust<br>set<br>up<br>by the<br>court<br>for<br>a<br>minor<br>or<br>incapacitated<br>person                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Ancillary and<br>Domiciliary<br>Trust<br>Returns                                 | A<br>trust<br>which<br>exists<br>in<br>a<br>foreign<br>state<br>because<br>the<br>grantor<br>is<br>domiciled<br>(resides)<br>in<br>another<br>state                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| Family Estate<br>Trust                                                           | A<br>trust<br>instrument<br>provides<br>evidence<br>of<br>ownership,<br>such<br>as<br>certificates<br>of<br>beneficial<br>interest<br>in<br>the<br>trust.<br>The<br>grantor<br>is<br>a<br>trustee<br>and<br>executive<br>officer;<br>and<br>The<br>corpus<br>and<br>undistributed<br>income<br>are<br>distributed<br>to<br>the<br>owners<br>after<br>the<br>trust<br>is<br>terminated.<br>Note:<br>This<br>is<br>also<br>known<br>as<br>a<br>family,<br>family estate,<br>pure,<br>equity,<br>equity pure,<br>prime,<br>or<br>constitutional<br>trust. |
| Generation<br>Skipping<br>Trust                                                  | A<br>trust<br>with<br>younger<br>generation<br>beneficiaries<br>who<br>are<br>more<br>than<br>one<br>generation<br>younger<br>than<br>the<br>grantor's<br>generation.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| Pooled<br>Income<br>Trust<br>(also<br>known<br>as<br>Split<br>Interest<br>Trust) | A<br>split<br>interest<br>trust<br>with<br>a:<br>Remainder<br>interest<br>for<br>a<br>public<br>charity,<br>and<br>Life<br>income<br>interest<br>retained<br>by<br>a<br>donor<br>or<br>for<br>another<br>person                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |

| Term                               | Definition                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|
| Clifford<br>Trust                  | A<br>grantor<br>type<br>trust<br>where<br>the<br>assets<br>are<br>placed<br>in<br>a<br>trust<br>but<br>there<br>is<br>still<br>some<br>ownership.<br>It<br>is<br>taxable<br>to<br>the<br>grantor.                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Non-Explicit<br>Trust              | An<br>arrangement<br>that<br>has<br>substantially the<br>same<br>effect<br>as<br>a<br>trust.<br>It<br>is<br>treated<br>as<br>a<br>trust<br>even<br>though<br>it<br>is<br>not<br>an<br>explicit<br>trust.<br>Non-explicit<br>trusts<br>do<br>not<br>include<br>the<br>decedent's<br>estate.<br>Examples:<br>Insurance<br>and<br>annuity contracts,<br>arrangements<br>involving<br>life<br>estates<br>and<br>remainders. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Non-exempt<br>Charitable<br>Trusts | A<br>trust<br>that<br>is<br>set<br>up<br>for<br>a<br>charitable<br>purpose<br>but<br>that<br>is<br>not<br>eligible<br>for<br>exempt<br>status                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

#### <span id="page-160-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.8.2 (06-06-2013)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Trusts**

- Established EINs can be disclosed to: (1)
  - A grantor (only when the trust is a grantor trust. See IRM 21.7.4.4.1.1.3, Types of Trusts, for more information on a grantor trust.)
  - A trustee
  - A beneficiary having a material interest (must be submitted in writing with proof of material interest, such as a copy of the will), or
  - An authorized representative
- EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)

#### <span id="page-160-1"></span>**21.7.13.5.8.3 (10-01-2024)**

### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Trusts**

<span id="page-161-0"></span>Use the table below to determine if an EIN is needed. (1)

> **Note:** A change of beneficiaries or trustee does not mean a new EIN is required.

<span id="page-161-1"></span>

| If                                        | Then                                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|-------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|
| 1)<br>A<br>new<br>trust<br>entity is      | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| created                                   |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 2)<br>The<br>trust<br>becomes             | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| irrevocable<br>following<br>death         |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 3)<br>An<br>estate<br>changes<br>to<br>a  | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| testamentary trust                        |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 4)<br>A<br>trust<br>changes<br>to<br>an   | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| estate                                    |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 5)<br>A<br>living<br>or<br>inter<br>vivos | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| trust<br>changes<br>to<br>a               |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| testamentary trust                        |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 6)<br>A<br>living<br>trust<br>is          | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                          |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| terminated<br>by distributing             |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| trust                                     |                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 7)<br>The<br>grantor/trustee<br>for<br>a  | An<br>EIN<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>but<br>may be                           |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| grantor<br>trust                          | assigned.<br>Inform<br>the<br>grantor/trustee                                 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Was<br>created<br>in<br>a<br>tax          | that<br>they must:                                                            |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| year<br>beginning<br>on<br>or             | Furnish<br>their<br>Social<br>Security                                        |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| after<br>January 1,<br>1981,              | Number<br>(SSN)<br>to<br>payers<br>of                                         |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| and                                       | income,<br>and                                                                |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Meets<br>specific<br>criteria             | Report<br>all<br>items<br>of<br>income,                                       |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| (see<br>Form<br>1041                      | deduction,<br>and<br>credit<br>from<br>the                                    |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| instructions)                             | trust<br>on<br>their<br>Form<br>1040.                                         |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|                                           | Note:<br>The<br>trust<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>to<br>file<br>Form<br>1041. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| If                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|--|
| 8)<br>A<br>grantor<br>trust<br>is<br>located<br>in<br>the<br>U.S.<br>and<br>has<br>all<br>assets<br>located<br>in<br>the<br>U.S.<br>and<br>either:<br>The<br>same<br>individual<br>is<br>both<br>grantor<br>and<br>trustee<br>(or<br>co<br>trustee)<br>of<br>the<br>trust,<br>or<br>The<br>individual<br>is<br>treated<br>as<br>the<br>owner<br>of<br>all<br>trust<br>assets<br>under<br>IRC<br>676<br>(power<br>to<br>revoke)<br>for<br>the<br>tax<br>year                   | An<br>EIN<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>but<br>may be<br>assigned.<br>Inform<br>the<br>grantor/trustee<br>that<br>they:<br>Must<br>furnish<br>their<br>SSN<br>to<br>payers<br>of<br>income,<br>and<br>Report<br>all<br>items<br>of<br>income,<br>deduction,<br>and<br>credit<br>from<br>the<br>trust<br>on<br>their<br>Form<br>1040. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 9)<br>A<br>revocable<br>trust<br>has:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         | Do<br>not<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Spouses<br>listed<br>as<br>the<br>sole<br>grantors<br>One<br>spouse<br>as<br>trustee<br>or<br>co-trustee<br>with<br>a<br>third<br>party<br>Both<br>spouses<br>as<br>trustee/co-trustee<br>with<br>a<br>third<br>party<br>One<br>or<br>both<br>spouses<br>treated<br>as<br>the<br>owners<br>of<br>all<br>trust<br>assets<br>under<br>IRC<br>676<br>for<br>the<br>tax<br>year,<br>or<br>Spouses<br>filing<br>a<br>joint<br>income<br>tax<br>return<br>for<br>the<br>tax<br>year | Instead,<br>inform<br>the<br>trustee<br>that<br>they<br>must:<br>Furnish<br>their<br>SSN<br>to<br>payers<br>of<br>income,<br>and<br>Report<br>all<br>items<br>of<br>income,<br>deduction,<br>and<br>credit<br>from<br>the<br>trust<br>on<br>their<br>Form<br>1040.                                                                 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

### **Questionable Trusts**

<span id="page-164-0"></span>

#### <span id="page-164-2"></span>**21.7.13.5.8.4 (04-23-2019)**

#### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: Trusts**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research a trust before assigning an EIN. (2)

<span id="page-165-2"></span><span id="page-165-1"></span><span id="page-165-0"></span>

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1    | Validate<br>the<br>grantor/trustor,<br>SSN,<br>ITIN,<br>or<br>EIN<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|      | CC<br>INOLE<br>CC<br>NAMEI<br>CC<br>NAMES<br>CC<br>NAMEE                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|      | Note:<br>If<br>you<br>are<br>unable<br>to<br>locate<br>or<br>validate<br>a<br>TIN,<br>contact<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>by phone,<br>fax,<br>or<br>mail<br>to<br>resolve<br>the<br>issue.                                                                                                                                         |
|      | Exception:<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>applications<br>(mailed/faxed)<br>with<br>a<br>received<br>date<br>of<br>May 13,<br>2019<br>and<br>subsequent<br>cannot<br>list<br>an<br>entity (EIN)<br>as<br>the<br>responsible<br>party.<br>The<br>responsible<br>party<br>must<br>be<br>an<br>individual<br>with<br>a<br>valid<br>SSN/ITIN. |
|      | Exception:<br>A<br>foreign<br>individual<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>to<br>have<br>an<br>ITIN,                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|      | but<br>the<br>EIN<br>will<br>still<br>be<br>assigned.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.3.2.7,<br>Foreign<br>Entities<br>-<br>Definitions<br>and<br>Instructions.                                                                                                                                                                      |
| 2    | Research<br>the<br>trust<br>name<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB<br>CC<br>NAMEE<br>CC<br>ENMOD,<br>and<br>CC<br>INOLE                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
|      | Example:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB:<br>Alabaster,<br>Mich<br>CC<br>NAMEE:<br>Mich]Alabaster<br>or<br>Alabaster<br>Mich<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                      |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                                                                                   |

#### <span id="page-165-4"></span><span id="page-165-3"></span>**21.7.13.5.8.5 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Trusts Filing as an Estate**

<span id="page-165-5"></span>If the entity type selected on Form SS-4 is trust or estate, establish the entity on BMF with a filing requirement of Form 1041. (1)

**Note:** This will generate a 6/7 million series number.

- The trust must have filing as an estate under IRC 645 entered in the Primary Name field on ESIGN. (2)
- (3) Trusts can file as estates under Treas. Reg. 1.645-1.

#### **21.7.13.5.8.6 (04-23-2019)**

#### **CC ESIGN Input: Trusts**

This subsection contains information about completing fields specific to a trust. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3, CC ESIGN Input Screen, for general input instructions. (1)

<span id="page-166-0"></span>

| Field               | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                           |
|---------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Master-File<br>Ind. | The<br>Master<br>File<br>indicator<br>(MFI)<br>is:                                                                                                           |
|                     | B<br>if<br>there<br>are<br>filing<br>requirements<br>input<br>on<br>ESIGN<br>O<br>if<br>there<br>are<br>no<br>filing<br>requirements<br>input<br>on<br>ESIGN |
|                     | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.3,<br>Master<br>File<br>Indicator<br>Input.                                                                                        |
| Loc-Cd              | Input<br>the<br>valid<br>two-digit<br>EIN<br>prefix<br>for<br>the<br>campus.                                                                                 |
|                     | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.2.4,<br>How<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Assigned.                                                                                            |
|                     | Note:<br>The<br>last<br>two<br>positions<br>of<br>the<br>field<br>display<br>the                                                                             |
|                     | Area<br>Office<br>Code<br>(00).                                                                                                                              |

<span id="page-167-2"></span><span id="page-167-1"></span><span id="page-167-0"></span>

| Field        | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                             |
|--------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Name-Ctrl    | Name<br>control<br>is<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>characters<br>of<br>an                                        |
|              | individual's<br>last<br>name.                                                                                  |
|              | Note:<br>Michael<br>I<br>Azal<br>ea<br>Trust,<br>enter<br>AZAL.                                                |
|              | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.8.6.1,<br>Exception<br>Name<br>Controls:                                               |
|              | Trusts,<br>for<br>exceptions<br>to<br>Trust<br>name<br>controls.                                               |
|              | For<br>more<br>information<br>on<br>inputting<br>Name<br>Control,<br>see                                       |
|              | Document<br>7071-A,<br>Name<br>Control<br>Job<br>Aid<br>-<br>For<br>Use                                        |
|              | Outside<br>of<br>the<br>Entity Area.                                                                           |
|              | Exception:<br>Trusts<br>established<br>via<br>the<br>internet<br>follow<br>corporate<br>name<br>line<br>rules. |
|              | -<br>The<br>system<br>cannot<br>distinguish<br>a<br>name<br>(first<br>or<br>last)                              |
|              | from<br>other<br>words<br>in<br>the<br>trust<br>name.                                                          |
|              | -<br>Taxpayers<br>are<br>provided<br>with<br>examples<br>showing<br>how                                        |
|              | to<br>enter<br>the<br>trust<br>name.                                                                           |
|              | -<br>The<br>application<br>will<br>move<br>specific<br>trust<br>noise                                          |
|              | phrases<br>to<br>the<br>end<br>of<br>the<br>primary name<br>line.                                              |
|              | However,<br>regardless<br>of<br>how<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>enters<br>the                                        |
|              | information,<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>valid<br>characters<br>entered<br>by                                   |
|              | the<br>taxpayer<br>establish<br>the<br>name<br>control.                                                        |
| Primary-Name | The<br>Primary Name<br>line<br>must<br>include<br>the<br>mandatory                                             |
|              | trust<br>abbreviations<br>listed.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.8.6.2,                                            |
|              | Mandatory Trust<br>Abbreviations<br>Primary Name:                                                              |
|              | Trusts.                                                                                                        |
|              | Note:<br>If<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>uses<br>a<br>different<br>abbreviation,                                      |
|              | enter<br>their<br>abbreviation.                                                                                |
|              |                                                                                                                |
|              | For<br>Estates<br>and<br>Trusts,<br>any information<br>in<br>the                                               |
|              | primary name<br>line<br>that<br>is<br>in<br>front<br>of<br>the<br>taxpayer's                                   |
|              | name<br>must<br>be<br>moved<br>behind<br>the<br>name.                                                          |
|              | Example:<br>Insurance<br>Trust<br>of<br>John<br>Doe                                                            |
|              | JOHN<br>DOE<br>INS<br>TR                                                                                       |

<span id="page-168-0"></span>

| Field          | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                  |
|----------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Sort-Name      | The<br>Sort<br>Name<br>is<br>always<br>the<br>individual<br>trustee's<br>or         |
|                | personal<br>representative's<br>name.<br>Enter<br>the<br>name<br>as                 |
|                | indicated<br>by the<br>taxpayer<br>followed<br>by TTEE.<br>If<br>there<br>is        |
|                | more<br>than<br>one<br>trustee<br>and<br>it<br>is<br>not<br>possible<br>to<br>enter |
|                | all<br>the<br>trustees<br>as<br>the<br>Sort<br>Name,<br>list<br>the<br>maximum      |
|                | number<br>of<br>names<br>and<br>add<br>the<br>phrase<br>ET<br>AL<br>TTEE.           |
|                | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.4.1,<br>Basic<br>Information<br>on<br>the               |
|                | Sort<br>Name<br>Input,<br>and<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.4.2,<br>Sort                  |
|                | Name<br>Input<br>Field<br>Requirements,<br>for<br>input                             |
|                | information.<br>Do<br>not<br>use<br>a<br>bank,<br>mortgage<br>company,              |
|                | or<br>corporation<br>as<br>the<br>Sort<br>Name.<br>Instead,<br>enter<br>it<br>as    |
|                | the<br>In-Care<br>of<br>Name.                                                       |
| Care-of-Name   | If<br>a<br>company is<br>the<br>trustee,<br>enter<br>the<br>company<br>name         |
|                | on<br>the<br>care<br>of<br>line<br>(as<br>indicated<br>by the<br>taxpayer),         |
|                | followed<br>by TTEE.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.5,<br>Care<br>of                |
|                | Name<br>Input,<br>for<br>input<br>information.                                      |
| Mail-Street-Or | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.2,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP       |
| Foreign        | Field,<br>for<br>input<br>requirements.                                             |
| City/Zip       | Note:<br>The<br>business<br>location<br>address<br>for<br>a<br>trust<br>can         |
|                | be<br>a<br>P.O.<br>Box.                                                             |
| Mail           | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.3,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP       |
| City/State/Zip | or<br>Foreign<br>Country Field,<br>for<br>input<br>requirements.                    |
| Or-Foreign     |                                                                                     |
| Country        |                                                                                     |
| Location       | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.4,<br>Location<br>Street<br>Address<br>Field,           |
| Street-Address | for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                       |
| Location       | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.5,<br>Location<br>City/State/ZIP<br>Input,              |
| City/State/Zip | for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                       |

<span id="page-169-2"></span><span id="page-169-1"></span><span id="page-169-0"></span>

| Field                  | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Filing<br>Requirements | Assign<br>FR<br>1041-1<br>to<br>Trusts<br>and<br>Estates.<br>(See<br>exceptions<br>below.)<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.9,<br>Filing<br>Requirements<br>Input.<br>If<br>employees<br>are<br>indicated,<br>establish<br>a<br>FR<br>1041-1<br>and<br>941-01<br>or<br>944-01<br>(if<br>appropriate)<br>and<br>940-1.<br>If<br>agricultural<br>employees<br>are<br>indicated,<br>establish<br>a<br>943<br>FR.                   |
|                        | Exception:<br>Do<br>not<br>establish<br>a<br>1041<br>FR<br>if<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>annotates<br>"Widely Held<br>Investment<br>Trust"<br>or<br>"IRC<br>1.671-5(b)(22)"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|                        | Exception:<br>If<br>taxpayer<br>annotates<br>Regulation<br>301.7701-4,<br>establish<br>a<br>FR<br>of<br>1065-1.<br>These<br>types<br>of<br>business<br>arrangements<br>are<br>not<br>classified<br>as<br>trusts<br>under<br>the<br>Internal<br>Revenue<br>Code.<br>Also<br>Common<br>Trust<br>Funds<br>under<br>IRC<br>584<br>are<br>assigned<br>Form<br>1065<br>filing<br>requirements.                                    |
| FYM                    | A<br>fiscal<br>year<br>month<br>(FYM)<br>must<br>be<br>entered<br>for<br>trusts<br>with<br>filing<br>requirements.<br>For<br>filing<br>requirement<br>1041,<br>enter<br>12<br>(December)<br>as<br>the<br>FYM.<br>Enter<br>FYM<br>of<br>12,<br>unless<br>taxpayer<br>cites<br>Treas.<br>Reg.<br>1.645-1(c).                                                                                                                  |
|                        | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.10,<br>Fiscal<br>Year Month<br>Input.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| XREF-TIN-Type          | SSN/ITIN<br>=<br>0<br>EIN<br>=<br>2<br>Exception:<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>applications<br>(mailed/faxed)<br>with<br>a<br>received<br>date<br>of<br>May 13,<br>2019<br>and<br>subsequent<br>cannot<br>list<br>an<br>entity (EIN)<br>as<br>the<br>responsible<br>party.<br>The<br>responsible<br>party must<br>be<br>an<br>individual<br>with<br>a<br>valid<br>SSN/ITIN.<br>Therefore<br>the<br>X-REF-TIN-Type<br>will<br>be<br>0. |

<span id="page-170-0"></span>

| Field                | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                            |
|----------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| SSN/ITIN/EIN         | Grantor's<br>X-REF<br>SSN/ITIN/EIN<br>from<br>Form<br>SS-4,<br>Line                           |
|                      | 7b<br>or<br>9a                                                                                |
|                      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.3.2.7,<br>Foreign<br>Entities<br>-<br>Definitions                       |
|                      | and<br>Instructions,<br>for<br>important<br>information<br>on                                 |
|                      | foreign<br>entities/persons.                                                                  |
|                      | Exception:<br>Form<br>SS-4<br>applications<br>(mailed/faxed)                                  |
|                      | with<br>a<br>received<br>date<br>of<br>May 13,<br>2019<br>and<br>subsequent                   |
|                      | cannot<br>list<br>an<br>entity (EIN)<br>as<br>the<br>responsible<br>party.                    |
|                      | The<br>responsible<br>party must<br>be<br>an<br>individual<br>with<br>a<br>valid<br>SSN/ITIN. |
| Business             | The<br>business<br>operational<br>date<br>(BOD)<br>is<br>the<br>later<br>of,                  |
| Operational          | the<br>date<br>the<br>trust<br>was<br>created<br>or<br>the<br>date<br>the<br>trust            |
| Date                 | was<br>funded.<br>If<br>none<br>is<br>provided<br>on<br>Line<br>11,<br>use<br>the             |
|                      | current<br>month<br>and<br>year.                                                              |
| Notice               | The<br>notice<br>information<br>code<br>(NIC)<br>is<br>a<br>required<br>field                 |
| Information-Cd       | only if<br>a<br>notice<br>other<br>than<br>CP<br>575<br>is<br>desired.                        |
|                      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.13,<br>Notice<br>Information<br>Code                                |
|                      | Input.                                                                                        |
| Reason               | The<br>reason<br>applied,<br>Form<br>SS-4,<br>Line<br>10,<br>is<br>used<br>when               |
| Applied              | the<br>MFI<br>is<br>B<br>or<br>O.                                                             |
|                      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.20,<br>Reason<br>Applied<br>Input,<br>for<br>a                      |
|                      | complete<br>list<br>of<br>Reason<br>Applied<br>Codes.                                         |
| Phone                | The<br>10<br>digit<br>telephone<br>number<br>of<br>the<br>grantor,                            |
|                      | fiduciary,<br>or<br>personal<br>representative.                                               |
| Prior-EIN            | If<br>the<br>MFI<br>is<br>B<br>and<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>applied<br>for<br>an<br>EIN<br>for   |
| Indicator            | either<br>this<br>or<br>another<br>business<br>(taxpayer<br>has<br>checked                    |

| Business             | County and<br>State<br>where<br>business<br>is<br>located.                                    |

| County and           |                                                                                               |
| State                |                                                                                               |
| Type<br>of<br>Entity | Input<br>"10"                                                                                 |
| Type<br>of<br>Entity | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.25,<br>Type<br>of<br>Entity and<br>Type<br>of                       |
| Remarks              | Entity Remarks<br>(Form<br>SS-4,<br>Line<br>9a).                                              |
| Reason<br>for        | Form<br>SS-4,<br>Line<br>10                                                                   |
| Applying             | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.26,<br>Reason<br>for<br>Applying<br>Message.                        |
| Message              |                                                                                               |

#### <span id="page-171-0"></span>**21.7.13.5.8.6.1 (10-01-2025)**

#### **Exception Name Controls : Trusts**

Use the table below to enter Name Control for exceptions to the trust Name Control rules. (1)

| If<br>the<br>trust                           | Then                                                               |
|----------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>Is<br>an<br>entity other<br>than       | Use<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>characters<br>of<br>the<br>entity's |
| an<br>individual                             | name.                                                              |
|                                              | Example:<br>Daisy Corp.<br>Employee<br>Benefit                     |
|                                              | Trust,<br>enter<br>DAIS.                                           |
| 2)<br>Is<br>a<br>GNMA<br>Pool                | Use<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>digits/alphas<br>of<br>the<br>trust |
|                                              | number,<br>disregarding<br>any leading<br>zeroes                   |
|                                              | or<br>trailing<br>alphas.<br>If<br>there<br>are<br>fewer<br>than   |
|                                              | four<br>digits<br>in<br>the<br>trust<br>number,<br>use<br>the      |
|                                              | letters<br>GNMA<br>or<br>FNMA.                                     |
|                                              |                                                                    |
|                                              | Example:<br>GNMA<br>Pool<br>0001,<br>enter<br>1GNM                 |
|                                              | and<br>GNMA<br>Pool<br>0100B,<br>enter<br>100G.                    |
| 3)<br>Is<br>a<br>split<br>interest<br>trust, | Use<br>trust<br>Name<br>Control<br>rules,<br>even<br>if<br>the     |
| and<br>files<br>Form<br>5227,<br>Split       | fund<br>or<br>foundation<br>is<br>part<br>of<br>the                |
| Interest<br>Information                      | organization's<br>name.                                            |
| Return                                       |                                                                    |

| If<br>the<br>trust                | Then                                                   |
|-----------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| 4)<br>Does<br>not<br>provide      | Use<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>characters<br>of<br>the |
| specific<br>trust<br>information  | beneficiary's<br>last<br>name.                         |
| such<br>as<br>corporate<br>name,  | Example:<br>Irrevocable<br>Trust<br>FBO<br>Laura       |
| grantor,<br>etc.                  | Chatfield,<br>enter<br>CHAT.                           |
| 5)<br>Organization's<br>name      | Use<br>trust<br>Name<br>Control<br>rules.              |
| contains<br>both<br>Trust/Fund    |                                                        |
| and<br>an<br>individual's<br>name |                                                        |

#### **21.7.13.5.8.6.2 (03-11-2014)**

### **Mandatory Trust Abbreviations Primary Name: Trusts**

- The following list contains mandatory abbreviations to be used when assigning an EIN to a trust: (1)
  - Administrator **ADM**
  - Dated Jan. 16, 1987 01161987

**Note:** Do not enter date/dated or the alpha month.

- Executor/Executrix **EX**
- Family **FAM**
- Fiduciary **FID**
- For the Benefit of, F/B/O, or F B O **FBO**
- Funeral **FNRL**
- Insurance **INS**
- Inter vivos **INTRVS**
- Irrevocable **IRRV**
- Marital **MRTL**
- Non-Exempt Charitable **NECT**
- Personal Representative **PER REP**
- Revocable **RVOC**
- Successor **SUCC**
- Testamentary **TEST**
- Trust **TR**
- Trustee **TTEE**
- Under agreement –Under agreement with U/A **UA**
- Under the will of Under will U/W **UW**
- Under Trust Agreement **UTA**
- Voluntary Employee Benefit Association **VEBA**

The table below contains procedures to obtain specific Name trust information: (2)

| Step | Action                                                                                                                    |
|------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1    | Contact<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>by telephone<br>to<br>obtain<br>the<br>missing                                              |
|      | information.                                                                                                              |
| 2    | Were<br>you<br>able<br>to<br>make<br>contact?                                                                             |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>this<br>ends<br>the<br>procedure.<br>If<br>no,<br>correspond<br>with<br>taxpayer<br>using<br>Letter<br>45C. |

#### **21.7.13.5.9 (03-02-2018)**

#### **EIN Assignment: Bankruptcy Estate**

This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for bankruptcy estates. (1)

#### **21.7.13.5.9.1 (05-17-2010)**

#### **Definition of a Bankruptcy Estate**

- A bankruptcy estate is a separate and distinct taxable entity from the individual debtor, created when an individual debtor files for bankruptcy under Chapter 7 or 11. When an individual files for bankruptcy under these chapters of the bankruptcy code, a separate estate is created consisting of property held by the debtor as of the beginning of the case. Under some circumstances, this estate also consists of property acquired by the debtor and the estate after commencement of the case. (1)
- The table below describes associated terms and types of bankruptcy estates: (2)

| Term    | Definition                                                                             |
|---------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Chapter | A<br>liquidating<br>bankruptcy case<br>in<br>which<br>the<br>debtor<br>turns<br>over   |
| 7       | all<br>non-exempt<br>property to<br>the<br>bankruptcy<br>trustee,<br>who               |
|         | then<br>converts<br>it<br>to<br>cash<br>for<br>distribution<br>to<br>the<br>creditors. |

| Term    | Definition                                                                                      |  |
|---------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| Chapter | A<br>reorganization<br>bankruptcy case<br>in<br>which<br>debtors                                |  |
| 11      | (individuals,<br>corporations,<br>or<br>partnerships)<br>are<br>allowed<br>to                   |  |
|         | restructure<br>(reorganize)<br>their<br>debts<br>rather<br>than<br>liquidating                  |  |
|         | their<br>business.<br>The<br>debtor<br>usually remains<br>in<br>possession<br>of                |  |
|         | the<br>assets<br>(called<br>a<br>debtor-in-possession<br>or<br>DIP)<br>and<br>has<br>all        |  |
|         | the<br>fiduciary duties<br>and<br>responsibilities<br>of<br>a<br>trustee.<br>A                  |  |
|         | trustee<br>can<br>be<br>appointed<br>by the<br>bankruptcy<br>court<br>if<br>the                 |  |
|         | creditor<br>can<br>show<br>cause.<br>A<br>debtor<br>may also<br>choose<br>to                    |  |
|         | liquidate<br>assets<br>in<br>a<br>Chapter<br>11<br>case.                                        |  |
| Chapter | Adjustments<br>of<br>Debts<br>of<br>a<br>Family Farmer<br>with<br>Regular                       |  |
| 12      | Annual<br>Income.<br>This<br>is<br>a<br>chapter<br>designed<br>to<br>enable<br>a                |  |
|         | debtor<br>who<br>is<br>a<br>family farmer<br>to<br>reorganize<br>rather<br>than                 |  |
|         | liquidate<br>his<br>or<br>her<br>farming<br>operation.<br>A<br>family<br>farm<br>can<br>be<br>a |  |
|         | sole<br>proprietor,<br>a<br>partnership,<br>or<br>a<br>closely<br>held<br>corporation.          |  |
|         | Under<br>Chapter<br>12,<br>a<br>trustee<br>is<br>appointed<br>by<br>the<br>U.S.<br>Trustee      |  |
|         | to<br>act<br>in<br>each<br>case.<br>The<br>debtor<br>proposes<br>a<br>plan<br>of                |  |
|         | reorganization<br>to<br>repay the<br>creditors.<br>The<br>bankruptcy<br>code                    |  |
|         | limits<br>the<br>amount<br>and<br>percentage<br>of<br>debt<br>allowed<br>under<br>this          |  |
|         | plan,<br>as<br>well<br>as<br>the<br>income<br>derived<br>from<br>farming<br>operations.         |  |
| Chapter | Adjustment<br>of<br>Debts<br>of<br>an<br>Individual<br>with<br>Regular<br>Income.               |  |
| 13      | Only individuals,<br>including<br>self-employed<br>individuals,<br>with                         |  |
|         | regular<br>income<br>may file<br>for<br>bankruptcy<br>under<br>this<br>chapter.                 |  |
|         | There<br>are<br>specific<br>limits<br>as<br>to<br>the<br>kind<br>and<br>amount<br>of<br>debt    |  |
|         | that<br>an<br>individual<br>may have<br>to<br>qualify.<br>In<br>Chapter<br>13,<br>the           |  |
|         | debtor<br>makes<br>regular<br>payments<br>to<br>creditors<br>through<br>the                     |  |
|         | trustee<br>under<br>this<br>plan.<br>The<br>debtor<br>has<br>three<br>to<br>five<br>years<br>in |  |
|         | which<br>to<br>execute<br>the<br>plan<br>and<br>pay off<br>creditors,<br>after<br>which         |  |
|         | they will<br>be<br>discharged<br>of<br>the<br>debt.<br>Chapter<br>13<br>petitions               |  |
|         | must<br>be<br>voluntary.                                                                        |  |

#### **21.7.13.5.9.2 (05-17-2010)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: Bankruptcy Estate**

- Established EINs can be disclosed to: (1)
  - The bankrupt individual
  - The trustee, or
  - An authorized representative

EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or a taxpayer signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)

#### **21.7.13.5.9.3 (05-17-2010)**

#### **Determining the Need for an EIN: Bankruptcy Estates**

Use the table below to determine if an EIN is needed. (1)

**Note:** A change of trustee does not mean a new EIN is required.

| If                                             | Then                                                        |
|------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>A<br>new<br>bankruptcy estate<br>has     | Assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                        |
| been<br>created<br>under<br>Chapter<br>7<br>or |                                                             |
| Chapter<br>11                                  |                                                             |
| 2)<br>A<br>new<br>bankruptcy estate<br>has     | Do<br>not<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.<br>A<br>bankruptcy        |
| been<br>created<br>under<br>Chapter<br>12      | estate<br>created<br>under<br>Chapter<br>12<br>or           |
| or<br>Chapter<br>13                            | Chapter<br>13<br>is<br>not<br>treated<br>as<br>a            |
|                                                | separate<br>entity for<br>tax<br>purposes.                  |
| 3)<br>A<br>new<br>bankruptcy estate<br>has     | Assign<br>an<br>EIN<br>to<br>each<br>bankrupt               |
| been<br>created<br>and<br>more<br>than<br>one  | individual.                                                 |
| individual's<br>name<br>is<br>listed<br>on     |                                                             |
| Line<br>1<br>of<br>the<br>Form<br>SS-4         |                                                             |
| 4)<br>A<br>corporation<br>is<br>in             | Do<br>not<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.<br>Change<br>or<br>add    |
| bankruptcy,<br>or<br>a<br>fiduciary is         | a<br>Sort<br>Name<br>to<br>show<br>the<br>receiver's,       |
| appointed<br>in<br>a<br>state<br>insolvency    | trustee's<br>or<br>debtor<br>in<br>possession's             |
| proceeding.                                    | name.                                                       |
| 5)<br>A<br>partnership<br>files<br>bankruptcy  | Do<br>not<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.<br>Add<br>a<br>Care<br>of |
|                                                | Name<br>to<br>show<br>the<br>receiver's,                    |
|                                                | trustee's<br>or<br>debtor<br>in<br>possession's             |
|                                                | name.                                                       |
| 6)<br>A<br>sole<br>proprietor<br>files         | Assign<br>an<br>EIN<br>for<br>a<br>bankruptcy               |
| bankruptcy                                     | estate.<br>Do<br>not<br>assign<br>another<br>sole           |
|                                                | proprietor<br>EIN<br>to<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>in            |
|                                                | bankruptcy.                                                 |

#### **21.7.13.5.9.4 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: Bankruptcy Estate**

Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 (1)

below when performing research.

When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research an EIN request before assigning a number. (2)

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1    | Validate<br>the<br>grantor<br>(bankrupt<br>individual),<br>SSN,<br>or<br>ITIN<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                    |
|      | CC<br>INOLE<br>CC<br>NAMEI<br>CC<br>NAMES<br>CC<br>NAMEE                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|      | Note:<br>If<br>you<br>are<br>unable<br>to<br>locate<br>or<br>validate<br>a<br>TIN,<br>contact<br>the<br>taxpayer<br>by phone,<br>fax,<br>or<br>mail<br>to<br>resolve<br>the<br>issue.                                                                      |
|      | Exception:<br>A<br>foreign<br>individual<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>to<br>have<br>an<br>ITIN,<br>but<br>the<br>EIN<br>will<br>still<br>be<br>assigned.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.3.2.7,<br>Foreign<br>Entities<br>-<br>Definitions<br>and<br>Instructions. |
| 2    | Research<br>the<br>bankruptcy estate<br>name<br>using:                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB<br>CC<br>NAMEE<br>CC<br>ENMOD,<br>and<br>CC<br>INOLE                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|      | Example:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB:<br>Alabaster,<br>Mich<br>CC<br>NAMEE:<br>Mich]Alabaster<br>or<br>Alabaster<br>Mich<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information.                                                                                   |
| 3    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN.                                |

#### **21.7.13.5.9.5 (04-23-2019)**

#### **CC ESIGN Input: Bankruptcy Estate**

This subsection contains information about completing fields specific to a bankruptcy estate. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3, CC ESIGN Input Screen, for general input instructions (1)

| Field                                           | Description<br>of<br>Input<br>Data                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Master-File<br>Ind.                             | The<br>Master<br>File<br>indicator<br>is<br>always<br>B.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| Loc-Cd                                          | Input<br>the<br>valid<br>two-digit<br>EIN<br>prefix<br>for<br>the<br>campus.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.2.4,<br>How<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Assigned<br>Note:<br>The<br>last<br>two<br>positions<br>of<br>the<br>field<br>display<br>the                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|                                                 | Area<br>Office<br>Code<br>(00).                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| Name-Ctrl                                       | The<br>Name<br>Control<br>is<br>the<br>first<br>four<br>characters<br>of<br>the<br>bankrupt<br>individual's<br>last<br>name.<br>For<br>more<br>information<br>on<br>inputting<br>Name<br>Control,<br>see<br>Document<br>7071-A,<br>Name<br>Control<br>Job<br>Aid<br>-<br>For<br>Use<br>Outside<br>of<br>the<br>Entity Area.                                                                                                                                                          |
| Primary -Name                                   | The<br>Primary Name<br>must<br>include<br>the<br>name<br>of<br>the<br>bankrupt<br>individual's<br>name<br>followed<br>by<br>"Bankruptcy Estate"<br>Example:<br>Michael<br>Alabaster<br>Bankruptcy Estate.<br>Note:<br>If<br>the<br>application<br>indicates<br>more<br>than<br>one<br>bankrupt<br>individual,<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN<br>for<br>each<br>bankrupt<br>individual.                                                                                                       |
| Sort-Name                                       | If<br>the<br>case<br>number<br>is<br>provided<br>on<br>Line<br>3<br>of<br>the<br>Form<br>SS-4,<br>input<br>the<br>case<br>number<br>on<br>the<br>sort<br>name<br>line.<br>If<br>the<br>case<br>number<br>is<br>not<br>provided,<br>place<br>the<br>trustee's<br>(if<br>an<br>individual)<br>name<br>on<br>the<br>sort<br>name<br>line<br>followed<br>by TTEE.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.4.1,<br>Basic<br>Information<br>on<br>the<br>Sort<br>Name<br>Input.                     |
| Care-of-Name                                    | If<br>a<br>case<br>number<br>has<br>been<br>input<br>on<br>the<br>sort<br>name<br>line,<br>input<br>the<br>trustee's<br>(if<br>an<br>individual)<br>name<br>on<br>the<br>care<br>of<br>name<br>line<br>followed<br>by TTEE.<br>If<br>the<br>trustee<br>is<br>a<br>company,<br>input<br>the<br>trustee's<br>name<br>on<br>the<br>care<br>of<br>name<br>line<br>followed<br>by TTEE.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.6.5,<br>Care<br>of<br>Name<br>Input,<br>for<br>input<br>information. |
| Mail-Street-Or<br>Foreign-City/Zip              | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.2,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP<br>Field,<br>for<br>input<br>requirements.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |

### **21.7.13.5.10 (03-02-2018)**

#### **EIN Assignment: Real Estate Mortgage Investment Conduit (REMIC)**

This subsection contains information on assigning EINs for a real estate mortgage investment conduit (REMIC). (1)

### **21.7.13.5.10.1 (10-01-2005)**

**Definition: REMIC**

- (1) A **REMIC** is a real estate mortgage investment conduit.
- Some associated terms for REMIC are: (2)
  - Mortgage trusts
  - Mortgage securities
  - Asset investors trusts

#### **21.7.13.5.10.2 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Individuals Authorized to Receive EINs: REMIC**

Use the table below to determine the individuals authorized to receive an EIN. (1)

| If<br>the<br>REMIC…          | Then<br>disclose<br>the<br>EIN<br>to…                                |
|------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------|
| 1)<br>Is<br>a<br>corporation | A<br>corporate<br>officer<br>or<br>an<br>authorized                  |
|                              | representative.                                                      |
| 2)<br>Is<br>a<br>trust       | The<br>trustee<br>or<br>an<br>authorized<br>representative.          |
| 3)<br>Has<br>only            | Any person<br>who<br>signs<br>Form<br>1066<br>of<br>the<br>entity    |
| segregated<br>pools          | owning<br>the<br>assets<br>of<br>the<br>REMIC<br>under<br>applicable |
| of<br>assets                 | state<br>law<br>or<br>an<br>authorized<br>representative.            |

EINs must not be disclosed to a third party without a valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or a signed Form SS-4. See IRM 21.7.13.3.5.4, Taking an EIN Telephone Application, step 7 for more information on third party disclosure. (2)

#### **21.7.13.5.10.3 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Determining the Need for an EIN: REMIC**

- (1) Each REMIC must have its own EIN.
- A corporation, partnership, trust, etc. cannot use its EIN. A new EIN must be issued. (2)
- A new EIN must be assigned if the account found during research has a filing requirement of Form 1041, Form 1065, Form 1120, etc. (3)

#### **21.7.13.5.10.4 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Research Before Assigning an EIN: REMIC**

- Use the IAT EIN Assignment Tool to research an EIN request before assigning a number. The tool accesses all the CC's shown in paragraph 2 below when performing research. (1)
- When the tool is unavailable, follow the steps in the table below to research a REMIC before assigning an EIN. (2)

| Step | Action                                                                |  |
|------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 1    | Determine<br>whether<br>the<br>REMIC<br>has<br>an<br>EIN,<br>using:   |  |
|      | CC<br>NAMEB,<br>and<br>CC<br>NAMEE.                                   |  |
|      | See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2,<br>Researching<br>Taxpayer<br>Information. |  |

| Step | Action                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |  |
|------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 2    | Did<br>you<br>find<br>an<br>EIN?                                                                                                                                                                                            |  |
|      | If<br>yes,<br>verify that<br>the<br>EIN<br>is<br>a<br>valid<br>number.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.4.2.4,<br>If<br>an<br>EIN<br>is<br>Found/Not<br>Found.<br>If<br>no,<br>proceed<br>to<br>ESIGN<br>to<br>assign<br>an<br>EIN. |  |

#### **21.7.13.5.10.5 (10-01-2017)**

### **Form 1066 REMIC Tax Return**

- Form 1066, U.S. Real Estate Mortgage Investment Conduit Income Tax Return, is filed to: (1)
  - Report the income, deductions, and gains/losses from the operation of a REMIC, and
  - Report and pay tax on net income from prohibited transactions
- An entity that elects to be treated as a REMIC for its first tax year and meets the requirements of IRC 860D(a) must file Form 1066. (2)

#### **21.7.13.5.10.6 (04-23-2019)**
