#### **21.7.13.7.3.6.5 (12-18-2015)**

#### **Care of Name Input**

- (1) Care of Name field is not a required field.
- Do not input a Care of Name: (2)
  - If the Primary Name or the Sort Name line is identical to the Care of Name, or
  - If it is determined that the Care of Name is that of a third party and there is no valid Form 2848, Form 8821, or taxpayer signed Form SS-4 that addresses other tax matters in addition to the Form SS-4.
- The table below describes field requirements for Care of Name. (3)

| In-Care<br>of<br>Name                 |                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|---------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Input                                 | Field<br>Requirements                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Number<br>of<br>characters<br>allowed | 35<br>characters<br>per<br>line                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Characters                            | Can<br>be:<br>Alpha<br>Numeric<br>Blank,<br>or<br>The<br>special<br>characters,<br>hyphen<br>(-)<br>or<br>ampersand<br>(&)<br>Any characters<br>following<br>two<br>or<br>more<br>sequential<br>blanks<br>are<br>invalid. |

Use the information in the table below to handle special circumstances when inputting field entries for the Care of Name. (4)

| Care<br>of<br>Name                                                                                                       |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Special                                                                                                                  |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Circumstances                                                                                                            | Instruction                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| Prefixes<br>such<br>as                                                                                                   | Delete<br>from<br>Care<br>of<br>Name.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Mr.<br>Dr.<br>Rev.                                                                                                       |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| Suffixes<br>such<br>as                                                                                                   | Do<br>not<br>delete<br>from<br>Care<br>of<br>Name.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| Jr.<br>Sr.<br>III<br>Ph.D.<br>Suffixes<br>such<br>as<br>Pres./president<br>(or<br>other<br>title)<br>CPA<br>Esquire/Esq. | Delete<br>from<br>Care<br>of<br>Name.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| Business<br>Name                                                                                                         | Do<br>not<br>delete<br>from<br>Care<br>of<br>Name.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| includes<br>Gen<br>Ptr,<br>TTEE,<br>MBR,<br>EX.                                                                          | Reminder:<br>ESIGN<br>will<br>allow<br>for<br>35<br>characters<br>to<br>be<br>input<br>on<br>the<br>in<br>care<br>of<br>line.<br>However,<br>the<br>IAT<br>EIN<br>Assignment<br>Tool<br>is<br>limited<br>to<br>33<br>characters.<br>This<br>is<br>done<br>to<br>allow<br>for<br>the<br>input<br>of<br>"%"<br>The<br>tool<br>will<br>simply stop<br>input<br>when<br>it<br>reaches<br>the<br>33<br>character<br>maximum.<br>Users<br>must<br>determine<br>how<br>best<br>to<br>abbreviate<br>the<br>input<br>to<br>ensure<br>the<br>name<br>provided<br>and<br>the<br>required<br>title<br>is<br>clear<br>and<br>understandable. |

### **21.7.13.7.3.7 (03-02-2018)**

#### **Address Field Input**

This subsection contains information on domestic and foreign addresses. (1)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.7.1 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Foreign Street Address Field**

- (1) Foreign Street Address is not a required field.
- The table below describes a Foreign Street Address. (2)

| Foreign<br>Street<br>Address<br>Input | Field<br>Requirements                                                                                                  |
|---------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Number<br>of<br>characters<br>allowed | 35<br>characters<br>per<br>line                                                                                        |
| First<br>character                    | Must<br>be<br>alpha<br>or<br>numeric                                                                                   |
| Subsequent<br>characters              | Can<br>be:<br>Alpha<br>Numeric<br>Blank,<br>or<br>The<br>special<br>characters,<br>hyphen<br>(-)<br>or<br>slash<br>(/) |

### **21.7.13.7.3.7.2 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Mail Street or Foreign City/ZIP Field**

- The Mail Street or Foreign City/ZIP is either a foreign city or the mailing street address. (1)
- The table below describes the field requirements for Mail Street or Foreign City/ZIP. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3.8, Address Formatting Guidelines, for address formatting guidelines. (2)

| Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP<br>Input | Field<br>Requirements                                                                                                  |
|------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Number<br>of<br>characters<br>allowed                | 35<br>characters<br>per<br>line                                                                                        |
| Characters                                           | Can<br>be:<br>Alpha<br>Numeric<br>Blank,<br>or<br>The<br>special<br>characters,<br>hyphen<br>(-)<br>or<br>slash<br>(/) |

#### **21.7.13.7.3.7.3 (03-02-2018)**

**Mail City/State/ZIP or Foreign Country Field**

This subsection contains information on the Mail City/State/ZIP or Foreign Country Field. (1)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.7.3.1 (03-28-2011)**

#### **Basic Information on the Mail City/State/ZIP or Foreign Country Field**

- (1) The Mail City/State/ZIP or Foreign Country field is a required field.
- The correct entry for the Mail City/State/ZIP or Foreign Country field is either a: (2)
  - Foreign country
  - City/State/ZIP or Major City Code/ZIP

### **21.7.13.7.3.7.3.2 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Foreign Country Input**

- When inputting a foreign country: (1)
  - a. Check to be sure information is entered in the Foreign Address line.
  - b. Do not abbreviate the country name.
  - c. Input the country in the city field followed by a comma (,) period (.). **Example:** CANADA,.
  - d. Leave the ZIP Code blank.
- See IRM 21.7.13.7.3.8.4, ESIGN Entity Input for Foreign Addresses, for examples of Foreign Address input. (2)

### **21.7.13.7.3.7.3.3 (10-01-2007)**

#### **Mail City/State/ZIP Input, Major City Codes Input, and Zip Code Information**

The table below describes the field requirements for Mail Street or Foreign City/ZIP. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3.8, Address Formatting Guidelines, for address formatting guidelines. (1)

| City<br>Name<br>Input | Field<br>Requirements       |
|-----------------------|-----------------------------|
| Number<br>of          | 3<br>to<br>22<br>characters |
| characters            |                             |
| allowed               |                             |

| City<br>Name<br>Input                              | Field<br>Requirements                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|----------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Characters<br>(except<br>the<br>last<br>character) | Can<br>be:<br>Alpha,<br>or<br>Blank                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| Last<br>character                                  | Last<br>character<br>must<br>be<br>a<br>comma<br>(,)<br>followed<br>immediately by the<br>State<br>Code.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.8.3,<br>Domestic<br>Foreign<br>Addresses,<br>for<br>Army<br>Post<br>Office<br>(APO)/<br>Fleet<br>Post<br>Office<br>(FPO)and<br>US<br>Territories<br>State<br>Codes. |

- Never abbreviate a city, unless using a Major City Code. A valid Major City Code can be used in place of the City and State names, and can be used by any campus. See Document 7475, State and Address Abbreviations, Major City Codes (MCCs), ZIP Codes and Countries for a listing of MCCs. (2)
- When inputting a Major City Code (3)
  - a. Follow the code with two commas (,,).
  - b. Input a ZIP Code.

**Example:** Input Fargo, North Dakota 58126 as **FA,,58126**

If not using an MCC, input a valid two-character State Code after the comma following the city. Input a space after the State Code and input the ZIP Code. (4)

**Example:** Cincinnati, OH 45202

- A ZIP Code must be five to nine numeric characters. A valid range for the first five characters is 00601 to 99999. Both the fourth and fifth digits cannot be 00. See Document 7475, State and Address Abbreviations, Major City Codes (MCCs), ZIP Codes and Countries for a list of valid State Codes and ZIP Codes. (5)
  - a. Do not enter a ZIP Code for a foreign address.
  - b. The ZIP Code entered must be valid for the State Code entered.
  - c. The computer automatically expands the nine digit mailing ZIP Code to 12 digits for TC 000, TC 014, and TC 019.
  - d. The Finalist Program expands the rest of the ZIP Codes to 12 digits.

### **Location Street Address Field**

- The Location Street Address is the physical location of a business. A business may have two addresses: the mailing address and the location address. (1)
- Formatting requirements are the same as those for the Mail Street or Foreign City ZIP line. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3.8, Address Formatting Guidelines. (2)

### **21.7.13.7.3.7.5 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Location City/State/ZIP Input**

Use the table below to input a City/State/ZIP Location address. (1)

| If<br>inputting a                                       | Then                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |  |  |
|---------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|
| 1)<br>Domestic<br>City/State/ZIP<br>Location<br>address | Follow<br>instructions<br>for<br>input<br>of<br>Mail<br>City/State/ZIP<br>or<br>Foreign<br>Country line<br>input.<br>(See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.7.3.7.3,<br>Mail<br>Street<br>or<br>Foreign<br>City/ZIP<br>or<br>Foreign<br>Country Field.)<br>Input<br>a<br>comma<br>between<br>the<br>State<br>field<br>and<br>the<br>ZIP<br>Code<br>field.<br>Caution:<br>Do<br>not<br>input<br>a<br>location<br>address<br>if<br>it<br>is<br>the<br>same<br>as<br>the<br>mailing<br>address.                                                                                                                    |  |  |
| 2)<br>Foreign<br>City/State/ZIP<br>Location<br>address  | Ensure<br>that<br>the<br>location<br>street<br>address<br>has<br>been<br>input<br>Input<br>a<br>location<br>city of<br>at<br>least<br>three<br>alpha<br>characters<br>Input<br>a<br>location<br>country of<br>at<br>least<br>three<br>alpha<br>characters<br>followed<br>by a<br>comma<br>(,)<br>in<br>the<br>location<br>state<br>field,<br>and<br>Input<br>a<br>period<br>(.)<br>in<br>the<br>location<br>Zip<br>Code<br>field.<br>Note:<br>To<br>delete<br>a<br>foreign<br>location<br>address,<br>input<br>two<br>dollar<br>signs<br>(\$\$)<br>in<br>the<br>first<br>two<br>positions<br>of |  |  |

#### **21.7.13.7.3.8 (03-02-2018)**

#### **Address Formatting Guidelines**

(1) This subsection contains information on address formatting guidelines.

#### **21.7.13.7.3.8.1 (03-02-2018)**

#### **Handling Domestic Mailing and Location Addresses**

This subsection contains information on handling domestic mailing and location addresses. (1)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.8.1.1 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Basic Information on Domestic Mailing and Location Addresses**

- Mail is delivered to the last street address immediately preceding the city, state and ZIP Code. (1)
- If both a location address and a mailing address are present, input the: (2)
  - Location address on the location address line, and
  - Location City, State and ZIP Code on the location City/State/ZIP line. See IRM 21.7.13.7.3.7.5, Location City/State/ZIP Input, for information on inputting the location City/State/ZIP line.
- To delete a location address, input two dollar signs (\$\$) in the first two positions of the Location Street Address using CC BNCHG. (3)

### **21.7.13.7.3.8.1.2 (12-12-2016)**

### **Guidelines for Inputting the Mailing or Location Street Address**

- Observe the guidelines below when inputting the mailing or location street address information: (1)
  - a. Do not leave a blank space between the house or building number and a suffix.

**Example:** Input "1234 B North Street" as "1234B North St."

- b. Always input a house or building number. Do not accept a building name in place of a numeric. Contact the taxpayer, if necessary.
- c. Always input items such as the suite, apartment number, or room number at the end of the street address line.
- d. Always input the street suffix such as street, drive, lane, or terrace, if present.
- e. Always include the street directional such as North (N), South (S), East (E), or West (W).
- f. Input fractions as a slash (/).
- g. If the address contains a hyphen (-) such as 289–01 MAIN ST, enter the hyphen as part of the address. When entering a hyphen in an

- address, do not leave a space before the hyphen.
- h. If the address contains a pound sign (#) such as 1532 MAIN ST #15, input as 1532 MAIN ST 15.
- i. If the address contains an abbreviation for "number" , such as No. 15 MAIN ST or Num 15 MAIN ST, input as 15 MAIN ST.
- j. Abbreviate the first direction and leave the second direction spelled out if there are two directions in a street address.

**Example:** Input "North South Main St." as "N South Main St."

- k. Change Rural Federal Delivery (RFD) and RD to RR. Delete any leading zeros.
- l. Substitute the word "and" for the ampersand (&).
- m. Convert decimals to fractions.

**Example:** Input "1.5 miles south of Hwy 19" as "1 1/2 miles south of Hwy 19" .

n. A Private Mailbox (PMB) must be entered at the end of the address, regardless of where it is shown. It should always be included with the street address. Example: Private Mailbox 3, 102 S. 38 should be entered as 102 S 38 PMB 3.

#### **21.7.13.7.3.8.1.3 (10-01-2005)**

#### **PO Box Numbers**

- (1) A Post Office (PO) Box is always the mailing address, if present.
- When changing the mailing address from a street address to a PO box number, retain the street address as a location address as an audit trail for locating taxpayers. (2)
- For trusts and estates only, if the taxpayer indicates the street address is the mailing address and the PO Box is the location address, leave the PO Box as the location address. (3)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.8.1.4 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Handling Incomplete Addresses**

If no street address or PO Box is provided by the taxpayer, input the word "Local" on the street address line. (1)

**Note:** This should only occur in very small towns.

If the city or state is missing or incomplete and the ZIP Code is present, research the ZIP Code Directory, numeric section, to determine the city (2)

and state. If the city or state cannot be determined from the available information, make one attempt to contact the taxpayer by phone. If contact cannot be made, destroy the EIN application using proper security guidelines.

- (3) If the ZIP Code is missing, research the ZIP Code Directory and enter the ZIP Code.
- (4) If the city is listed as a major city, the Major City Code can be input in place of the city and state information on the mailing address and location address.
- (5) For information on State Abbreviations, Major City Codes and Address Abbreviations, see Document 7475, State and Address Abbreviations, Major City Codes (MCCs), ZIP Codes and Countries.

#### 21.7.13.7.3.8.2 (12-10-2014)

#### **Street Address Abbreviations**

(1) **Always** use the following street address abbreviations.

**Exception:** Abbreviate East, North, South, and West <u>only</u> when it is used as a direction of a street, avenue, etc. Also, never abbreviate street names such as "222 Second St.," "22 Third St.", or "1110 Boulevard Ln." that are spelled out by the taxpayer.

| Word                | Abbreviation | Word                          | Abbreviation                                                     |
|---------------------|--------------|-------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Air Force Base      | AFB          | Northeast                     | NE                                                               |
| Apartment           | APT          | Northwest                     | NW                                                               |
| Avenue              | AVE          | One-fourth, one-<br>half etc. | <sup>1</sup> / <sub>1</sub> , <sup>1</sup> / <sub>1</sub> , etc. |
| Boulevard           | BLVD         | Parkway                       | PKY/PKWY                                                         |
| Building            | BLDG         | Place                         | PL                                                               |
| Care of             | %            | Post Office Box               | PO BOX                                                           |
| In care of          | %            | Road                          | RD                                                               |
| Circle              | CIR          | Room                          | RM                                                               |
| Court               | СТ           | Rural Route                   | RR                                                               |
| Department          | DEPT         | Route                         | RT                                                               |
| Drive               | DR           | Rural Delivery                | RR                                                               |
| East                | Е            | South                         | S                                                                |
| Floor               | FL           | Southeast                     | SE                                                               |
| General<br>Delivery | GEN DEL      | Southwest                     | SW                                                               |
| Highway             | HWY          | Street                        | ST                                                               |

| Word     | Abbreviation | Word    | Abbreviation |
|----------|--------------|---------|--------------|
| Highway  | HC           | Suite   | STE          |
| Contract |              |         |              |
| Lane     | LN           | Terrace | TER          |
| North    | N            | West    | W            |

- Plurals for street, road, avenue, etc., will be entered as STS, RDS, AVES, etc. (2)
- If additional address abbreviations are needed to fit the 35 character limit, see USPS Acceptable Address Abbreviations in Section 4 of Document 7475, State and Address Abbreviations, Major City Codes (MCCs), ZIP Codes and Countries (3)

### **21.7.13.7.3.8.3 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Domestic Foreign Addresses**

- This subsection contains information on domestic foreign addresses, including: (1)
  - APO/FPO State Codes and
  - Territories and possessions State Codes.

### **21.7.13.7.3.8.3.1 (10-01-2014)**

#### **Army Post Office (APO)/Fleet Post Office (FPO)State Codes**

The table below lists the state codes that must be used in place of the city and state. (1)

| Geographic<br>Location | State<br>Code | Zip<br>Code         |
|------------------------|---------------|---------------------|
| Americas               | AA            | 340nn               |
| Europe                 | AE            | 090nn<br>-<br>098nn |
| Pacific                | AP            | 962nn<br>-<br>966nn |

Always enter "APO" and "FPO" in the address. The APO/FPO addresses are not considered foreign addresses and cannot be assigned the EIN prefix "66" , which is used for domestic foreign addresses. APO or FPO addresses must be transcribed with the correct two-character state code followed by the corresponding unique five-digit ZIP code. When APO or FPO is used, do not enter any other data in the city field. See the table below for instructions on entering these addresses on CC ESIGN: (2)

| If<br>the<br>address<br>is              | Enter<br>on<br>CC<br>ESIGN<br>as |
|-----------------------------------------|----------------------------------|
| APO<br>New<br>York<br>NY,<br>091nn      | APO<br>AE<br>091nn               |
| FPO<br>San<br>Francisco,<br>CA<br>962nn | FPO<br>AP<br>962nn               |

### **21.7.13.7.3.8.3.2 (11-18-2024)**

### **Territories and Possessions State Codes**

The table below lists the territories and possessions that are not entered as foreign addresses and require a valid State Code and Zip Code. If an EIN request (mail or fax) is received from one of the territories listed below, refer the case to the Cincinnati campus for processing. The EIN prefix is "66" . (1)

**Note:** EIN international phone calls from foreign entities are worked by Cincinnati and Ogden. If a call is received in a location other than Cincinnati or Ogden, provide the caller with the:

EIN International phone number (267) 941-1099 (not a toll-free number) and hours of operation 6:00 a.m. to 11:00 p.m. Eastern Time Monday through Friday and/or

Fax number (855) 215-1627 if faxing within the U.S. or (304) 707-9471 if faxing from outside the U.S.

| Country                                 | State<br>Code | Zip<br>Code               |
|-----------------------------------------|---------------|---------------------------|
| American<br>Samoa                       | AS            | 96799                     |
| Federated<br>States<br>of<br>Micronesia | FM            | 969nn                     |
| Guam                                    | GU            | 969nn                     |
| Northern<br>Mariana<br>Islands          | MP            | 969nn                     |
| Palau                                   | PW            | 969nn                     |
| Puerto<br>Rico                          | PR            | 006nn,<br>007nn,<br>009nn |
| U.S.<br>Virgin<br>Islands               | VI            | 008nn                     |

#### **21.7.13.7.3.9 (11-18-2024)**

### **Filing Requirements Input**

- A filing requirement is used to identify the type of return required to be filed by the taxpayer. If a taxpayer is required to file a return and does not, this input is used to perform a delinquency check. (1)
- Whenever an account is established on the BMF (that is, when the Master File Indicator is "B" ), it must have a filing requirement established. (2)
- This subsection contains input requirements for the various filing requirement fields on the CC ESIGN screen. (3)

### **21.7.13.7.3.9.1 (02-20-2013)**

#### **Form 941 Filing Requirement Input**

A Form 941, Employers QUARTERLY Federal Tax Return (Withholding and FICA Taxes) filing requirement indicates that a taxpayer is required to file this tax return. (1)

The table below identifies valid codes for a Form 941 filing requirement, as well as any additional requirements: (2)

| Filing Requirement                                                                       | Code | Other<br>Requirements                                                                                                                                                                                               |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Form<br>941<br>(other<br>than<br>Employment<br>Code<br>"F"<br>)<br>required<br>quarterly | 01   | Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>1<br>Exception:<br>A<br>Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>for<br>Employment<br>Codes<br>"G"<br>or<br>"W."                      |
| Form<br>941<br>required<br>quarterly for<br>Employment<br>Code<br>"F"                    | 02   | Employment<br>Code<br>must<br>be<br>"F,"<br>and<br>Form<br>940<br>and<br>Form<br>943<br>filing<br>requirements<br>must<br>be<br>blank.                                                                              |
| Form<br>941-SS<br>(Virgin<br>Islands,<br>Guam,<br>and<br>American<br>Samoa)              | 06   | Location<br>Code<br>must<br>be<br>6600<br>Form<br>940<br>must<br>be<br>blank                                                                                                                                        |
| Form<br>941-PR<br>(Puerto<br>Rico)                                                       | 07   | Location<br>Code<br>must<br>be<br>6600<br>,<br>and<br>Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>7.                                                                                                      |
|                                                                                          |      | Exception:<br>A<br>Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>is<br>not<br>valid<br>for<br>employment<br>code<br>"F."                                                                                                  |
| 941M<br>(civil<br>filer)<br>required<br>monthly                                          | 10   | Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>1<br>or<br>2.<br>Exception:<br>A<br>Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>is<br>not<br>required<br>for<br>employment<br>codes<br>"G,"<br>"W,"<br>or<br>"T." |

#### **21.7.13.7.3.9.2 (03-11-2014)**

#### **Form 940 Filing Requirement Input**

- A Form 940 filing requirement indicates that a taxpayer is required to file an Employers Annual Federal Unemployment Tax Return. (1)
- The table below identifies valid codes for a Form 940 filing requirement, as well as any additional requirements: (2)

| Filing                                        |      |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|-----------------------------------------------|------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Requirement                                   | Code | Other<br>Requirements                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| Form<br>940<br>required                       | 1    | Form<br>941<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>01,<br>and<br>Wages<br>Paid<br>Date<br>must<br>be<br>input.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|                                               |      | Exception:<br>A<br>Home<br>Care<br>Service<br>Recipient<br>(HCSR),<br>using<br>a<br>Household<br>Employer<br>(Fiscal)<br>Agent<br>under<br>IRC<br>3504<br>may have<br>a<br>Form<br>940<br>filing<br>requirement<br>without<br>a<br>corresponding<br>Form<br>941.<br>However,<br>this<br>is<br>not<br>an<br>issue<br>during<br>EIN<br>assignment<br>as<br>the<br>HCSR<br>is<br>established<br>initially with<br>no<br>filing<br>requirements.<br>See<br>IRM<br>21.7.13.5.15,<br>Home<br>Care<br>Service<br>Recipients<br>(HCSRs). |
| Form<br>940<br>Indian<br>Tribal<br>Government | 3    | Form<br>941<br>or<br>Form<br>944<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>01,<br>or<br>Form<br>943<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>1.<br>Wages<br>Paid<br>Date<br>must<br>be<br>input.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| Form<br>940-PR<br>(Puerto<br>Rico)            | 7    | Location<br>Code<br>must<br>be<br>6601.<br>Form<br>941<br>filing<br>requirement<br>must<br>be<br>07,<br>and<br>Wages<br>Paid<br>Date<br>must<br>be<br>input.<br>Note:<br>If<br>an<br>English<br>language<br>return<br>is<br>filed,<br>input<br>1.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

#### **21.7.13.7.3.9.10 (10-01-2010)**

### **Form 720 Filing Requirement Input**

- A Form 720 filing requirement indicates that a taxpayer is required to file a Quarterly Federal Excise Tax Return. (1)
- Excise taxes are taxes paid when purchases are made on a specific good, such as gasoline or tanning bed services. Excise taxes are often included in the price of the product. There are also excise taxes on activities, such as on wagering or on highway usage by trucks. (2)
- The table below identifies valid codes for a Form 720 filing requirement. **Note:** A filing requirement of Form 720 is valid with all other filing requirements. (3)

| Filing Requirement                        | Code                                       |  |
|-------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------|--|
| Form<br>720<br>required<br>quarterly.     | 1                                          |  |
| Form<br>720<br>casual<br>filer.<br>Return | 4                                          |  |
| not<br>required<br>quarterly.             | This<br>filing<br>requirement<br>is<br>not |  |
|                                           | assigned<br>during<br>Form<br>SS-4         |  |
|                                           | processing.                                |  |

### **21.7.13.7.3.10 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Fiscal Year Month Input**

- The fiscal year month (FYM) is a required field only for filing requirements 1041, 1065, or 1120. (1)
- (2) The FYM is the month in which the fiscal year of the entity ends.
- The values for this field are 01 12, with each number corresponding to a month. (3)

**Example:** 01 for January, 02 for February, 03 for March, etc.

#### **21.7.13.7.3.12 (03-02-2018)**

#### **Miscellaneous Fields Input**

This subsection contains information about the input of miscellaneous fields on ESIGN. (1)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.12.1 (10-01-2005)**

#### **FTD Suppression Indicator**

- The Federal Tax Deposit (FTD) suppression indicator is not an input field. It is generated based on the type of form the taxpayer is required to file. (1)
- (2) The Master File indicator must be B.

#### **21.7.13.7.3.12.2 (07-19-2010)**

#### **Cross Reference (XREF) TIN Type Input**

- In cross reference (XREF) TIN type, enter: (1)
  - **0** if a SSN/ITIN has been provided
  - **2** if an EIN has been provided
  - 9 if no SSN/ITIN/EIN will be entered into the SSN/ITIN/EIN field or no SSN will be entered into the Sole Proprietor SSN field when establishing a Sole Proprietorship. Continue to follow established guidance throughout this IRM to determine if a cross reference TIN is needed.

#### **21.7.13.7.3.12.3 (10-01-2022)**

**SSN/ITIN/EIN Input-XREF Responsible Party (Form SS-4, Line 7)**

- (1) The SSN/ITIN/EIN is required if a XREF TIN type is entered.
- Enter the nine digit cross reference SSN/ITIN or EIN. **Exception:** If the applicant has indicated they are Amish, a cross reference SSN or ITIN is not required. (2)
- Lines 7a and 7b of Form SS-4 must contain the name and TIN of the responsible party for all entity types. **Exception:** Sole Proprietors may provide their SSN/ITIN on line 9a. Responsible parties who do not have or are ineligible to obtain an SSN or ITIN may leave line 7b blank or notate "N/A" , "Foreign" , or similar language. (3)
- The **responsible party** is the person who ultimately owns or controls the entity or who exercises ultimate effective control over the entity. The person identified as the responsible party should have a level of control over, or entitlement to, the funds or assets in the entity that, as a practical matter, enables the person, directly or indirectly, to control, manage, or direct the entity and disposition of its funds and assets. **Unless the applicant is a government entity the responsible party must be an individual (i.e., a natural person), not an entity.** (4)
  - For entities with shares or interests traded on a public exchange, or which are registered with the Securities and Exchange Commission, "responsible party" is (a) the principal officer, if the entity is a corporation; or (b) a general partner, if a partnership. The general requirement that the responsible party be an individual applies to these entities. For example, if a corporation is the general partner of a public traded partnership for which Form SS-4 is filed, then the responsible party for the partnership is the principle officer of the corporation.
  - For tax-exempt organizations, the responsible party is generally the same as the principal officer as defined in the Form 990 instructions.
  - For government entities, the responsible party is generally the agency or agency representatives in a position to legally bind the particular government entity.
  - For trusts, the responsible party is a grantor, owner, or trustor.
- The IRS became aware of the use of nominees in the EIN application process. A nominee is temporarily authorized to act on behalf of entities during the business formation process in an effort to conceal the true (5)

**responsible party** of the newly created entity. The use of nominees in the EIN application process prevents us from gathering appropriate information on entity ownership and has been found to facilitate tax non-compliance by entities and their owners.

- The term **responsible party** will only be used when assigning an EIN by phone, fax or mail programs. It will not be used for disclosure purposes. You must follow normal disclosure procedures. (6)
- If you discover during a phone call that the taxpayer does not know what a responsible party means, ask the caller for the individual that controls, manages, or directs the applicant entity and the disposition of its funds and assets. Enter the SSN or ITIN of that owner into the SSN/ITIN/EIN field. If the taxpayer still does not know who that person will be, advise the caller to call back once they have determined who the responsible party is. You can also ref the caller to the instructions to the Form SS-4 which provide a definition of responsible party that is specific to different types (corporations, partnerships, trusts, etc.) (7)

### **21.7.13.7.3.12.4 (12-27-2012)**

### **Sole Proprietor SSN Input**

- The sole proprietor SSN/ITIN is a required field if: (1)
  - The entity is a Sole Proprietor
  - The MFI is B or O, and
  - 1041, 1065, 1120 and CT-1 filing requirements are not present **Note:** To delete an erroneously input Sole Proprietor SSN, input 000-00-0001 in this field using CC BNCHG.

**Note:** To correct a wrong SSN, input the correct Sole Proprietor SSN using CC BNCHG.

**Exception:** If the applicant has indicated they are Amish, a cross reference SSN or ITIN is not required.

You must check for a date of death prior to assigning an EIN. See IRM 21.7.13.2.2.3 Date of Death Check - Requirement for Responsible Party for Certain Entity Types - Online/Phone/Fax/Mail. (2)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.12.5 (10-01-2005)**

#### **Non-resident Alien Input**

- An entry in the non-resident alien field is only a required field when a Form 1042 filing requirement is present. (1)
- The table below describes field requirements for non-resident alien. (2)

| Non-resident<br>Alien<br>Input            | Field<br>Requirements                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|-------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Number<br>and<br>type<br>of<br>characters | Entry must<br>be<br>six<br>numerics<br>in<br>MMYYYY<br>format.<br>MM<br>must<br>equal<br>01-12.<br>The<br>YYYY<br>must<br>be<br>greater<br>than<br>1913<br>but<br>not<br>greater<br>than<br>current<br>year<br>plus<br>one. |

### **21.7.13.7.3.12.6 (10-01-2006)**

#### **Railroad Retirement Board Number Input**

- The Railroad Retirement Board Number is only a required field when CT-1 filing requirement is a 1 or a 2. (1)
- (2) The entry for this field must be 8 numerics.
- Generally, the EIN Assignment function will not have the information available for this input. (3)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.13 (10-01-2020)**

#### **Notice Information Code Input**

The notice information code (NIC) is a required field only if a notice other than CP 575 is desired. (1)

**Note:** The CP 575 applies to EIN assignments input when only an application has been received.

See IRM 3.13.2.8.2, Processing BMF Returns, for additional information about NIC codes and the notices generated from their input. (2)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.14 (10-01-2020)**

#### **Return Identity Code Input**

The Return Identity Code (RIC) is only required for accounts with Notice Information Codes A, B, J, P, and R. This information is recorded on the taxpayer notice. (1)

**Note:** Generally, Accounts Management only assigns EINs based on submission of Form SS-4 or an EIN application received over the phone.

- BMF Entity, EO Entity, and EPMF Entity use the RIC when EIN assignment is required to process a tax return or information document.
- The RIC field identifies the return or document causing the new EIN to be assigned. See IRM 3.13.2.8.2, Processing BMF Returns, for additional information about RIC codes. (2)

### **21.7.13.7.3.14.1 (10-01-2006)**

### **Return Identity Codes for Specific Notice and Master File Indicators Input**

The table below describes field input requirements for valid return identity codes for specific notice and Master File indicators: (1)

| If<br>the<br>notice<br>information<br>code<br>is | And<br>the<br>Master<br>File<br>indicator<br>is | Then<br>enter<br>Return<br>Identity<br>Code<br>must<br>be                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |  |
|--------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|

#### **21.7.13.7.3.18 (10-01-2008)**

#### **Duplicate Address Input**

(1) The duplicate address is not a required field.

An "N" in this position indicates the In Care of Name Line, the Mailing Street Address and the Mailing City, State and Zip Code on the current screen should be saved to a temporary file. Input of a "Y" indicates the information saved to the temporary file from the previous screen should be used for the current screen. (2)

#### **21.7.13.7.3.19 (10-01-2006)**

#### **Number of Employees Input**

- Employees is a required field only if the taxpayer indicates employees on Form SS-4, Line 13. (1)
  - **Exception:** If a taxpayer, other than a trust, indicates a Wages Paid Date on line 15, but leaves Line 13 blank, assign Form 941 and Form 940 filing requirements.
- This field is a five digit number indicating the number of employees that are employed by the business. (2)

- The Reason for Applying box must be completed by the taxpayer (for a paper or fax application) and entered by the assistor. (2)
- If the Reason for Applying box is not completed, contact the taxpayer or return the form as incomplete. (3)

### **21.7.13.7.3.24 (10-01-2016)**

#### **Business Location Input**

- Business location is a required entry for all domestic entities and has two fields of input: (1)
  - Business location county
  - Business location state

**Exception:** For domestic entities (formed or organized in the U.S. or U.S. territories) that only list a foreign mailing and/or location address, input the State, if provided, from line 9b of Form SS-4 in the business location state and leave the business location county blank. If nothing is provided on line 9b, leave both fields blank.
